Italian Fascist Party Newspaper 67

Discusses the Far Eastern Situation

European Countries Cannot Remain Unaffected by a Russo-Japanese Conflict

Past History Can Serve as a Lesson

Rome The Labor Newspaper of the Fascist Party published an article discussing Germany and the Far Eastern issue, stating that in the current situation, there is more than one factor that could disrupt peace in the Far East. For example, the conflict between Soviet Russia and "Manchukuo," Russian exiles engaging in disturbances with Japanese support, and the rumors of Anglo-Japanese consultations are all such factors. Although the Anglo-Japanese consultations cannot be completely believed, they can at least represent a rapprochement between the two countries. In short, Europeans should know that if a war breaks out between Russia and Japan, then Soviet Russia will no longer be able to concern itself with European affairs. If Soviet Russia does not have time to look westward, then Europe will be affected by this. This can be known from the past events of the Russo-Japanese War in 1904. At that time, the Russians poured all their efforts into Manchuria, and Germany and Austria took advantage of this, leading to the Tangier crisis in Africa and the Bosnian crisis in Central Europe. In 1904, the Anglo-French Entente was concluded. France recognized Britain's position in Egypt, and Britain also recognized France's special rights in Morocco. Germany was deeply jealous of this, but fearing the strength of the Russo-French alliance, it dared not easily launch an attack. By the end of 1904, the Russian army had suffered successive defeats, and Port Arthur was about to fall. The German Emperor then seized the opportunity and sought to share the benefits of Morocco with the French. On March 30, 1905, the German Emperor personally visited the port of Tangier in Morocco on a warship and issued a declaration stating that his arrival was to protect Germany's rights in Morocco. The momentum was fierce, and the international atmosphere was extremely tense for a time. If the Russian army had not been defeated at that time, the German Emperor's attitude would certainly not have been like this. The Bosnian crisis also occurred after Russia was defeated by Japan. The lands of Bosnia and Herzegovina originally belonged to Turkey. The Treaty of Berlin in 1878 stipulated that Austria should temporarily govern them, but sovereignty still belonged to Turkey. In October 1908, the Vienna government violated the treaty and announced the annexation of the two provinces to Austria. Although Turkey and Russia resolutely protested, it was to no avail. The reason why Austria dared to do so was also because Russia had just been defeated by Japan, the government was facing difficulties, and its military strength was weak. Although it did not approve, it did not have the practical strength to oppose it either. Both of these events are sufficient to serve as a lesson. The National Socialist Party of Germany's hope for serious Russo-Japanese relations is clearly visible. We sincerely hope that peace-loving countries will learn from the lessons of history, be able to calculate the consequences of their actions, and act accordingly to prevent such events from happening. (Havas Dispatch on the 3rd)

French Air Defense 68

Paris Is in Considerable Danger of Being Attacked

500 Airplanes in a Large-Scale Exercise

Winning the Attack in Two Hours

Germany Resumes Air Force Movement

Le Puy, France The air force exercise was completed at 11:00 AM this morning. This morning, the Blue Aircraft Team re-attacked the Le Puy airfield and various railway stations. According to the General Staff Department's judgment, the Blue Aircraft Team, due to its strong equipment and suitable climate, achieved victory as expected. This exercise determined that the aircraft equipment was satisfactory. Of the 500 airplanes that participated in the exercise, only two lost their combat capabilities. This exercise gained some useful experience for both sky offensive and defensive strategies. (Havas Dispatch on the 31st)

(Paris) The French air force exercise began today. The enemy aircraft team attacked Paris and the Le Bourget airfield for two hours, achieving considerable victory. Forty-eight enemy heavy bombers attacked the Le Bourget Allied airfield with flash bombs, reportedly rendering the airfield "destroyed" in theory. At the same time, Paris also suffered heavy damage. The enemy aircraft all escaped the observation posts. By the time the defending aircraft went into battle, the enemy aircraft had already flown back to their base. However, the anti-aircraft artillery team claimed that in a real air battle, they would have shot down several enemy aircraft. According to the opinions of experts who watched the battle, the defending forces suffered a severe attack. (Reuters Dispatch on the 30th)

(Paris) The air force held an exercise, attacking Paris. Although the weather was bad, 500 airplanes flew in the sky, colliding with each other without any accidents. Most of the bombers broke through the defense line. According to tactical calculations, it seemed that the Le Bourget airfield near Paris had been bombed twice. Some people believe that if it were a real battle, about half of the attacking airplanes would be shot down before reaching their target. The Morning Post said that the air force commander was satisfied with the strategic and technical results obtained from the exercise. The Echo de Paris believed that if the enemy suddenly attacked with a large number of airplanes, there would be no way to stop them. Therefore, it is necessary to always have a strong air force to fight in the air and seek victory. Former Aviation Minister Côte also published an article in the Enterprise News, saying that there are only three ways to prevent air warfare from being harmful: (1) abolish all military aviation, (2) establish an international supervisory organization to monitor the commercial aviation of various countries, and (3) create an international air force. The People's News stated that previous tests in foreign countries have proved that there is no way to prevent the enemy from attacking from the air. The French exercise has further confirmed this statement. (Havas Dispatch on the 31st)

(Geneva) The International Federation's Newspaper, the organ of the German International Federation Problems Research Association, still exists after Germany withdrew from the League of Nations. One page depicted a French air force squadron flying eastward, with the French caption "They have set off." The full text discussed "air danger, the development of the air force after the European War, and the French air force weapons and air force, etc." Attached were maps and models of French airplanes after 1932 as evidence. The article stated that other countries have huge air forces, while Germany has nothing. Its conclusion stated that, for the present, there are only two paths to follow: either all countries should abolish their air forces as soon as possible and destroy air force weapons, or Germany must follow the example of other countries and also demand the right to establish an air force to strengthen national defense. Germany is now in danger of being attacked from the air and cannot defend itself. For the sake of the people and the safety of the country, this situation cannot last. The article included several maps of Germany, with its western border still in the state before the European War. (Havas Dispatch on the 30th)

American Textile Industry Today 77

Begins a Major Strike

Involving 600,000 Workers

(Washington) All efforts to salvage the nationwide textile industry strike have failed as of today. National Labor Board Chairman Garrison announced that there is still no way to resolve the strike after consulting with Cotton Textile Association President Sloane and United Textile Workers of America Vice President Gorman. Garrison continued to say that the worker leaders rejected the truce proposal and did not want a joint investigation by the National Recovery Administration, the Labor Department, and the National Labor Board. Gorman declared that the union did not want to use riots to force factories to close and has notified workers to maintain order, not to approach the Communist Party, and to suppress Communist Party demonstrations. Regarding the resolution of the dispute, Gorman stated that if the factories cannot make substantial concessions to our demands, then we really have no way. It is now known that the major strike has been decided to begin at 11:30 AM on Saturday. The union ordered 600,000 textile workers nationwide this morning to go on strike on schedule. The strike was originally scheduled to begin today, but was finally postponed to Saturday. The three conditions put forward by the union workers are as follows: (1) changing the weekly 40-hour workweek to a weekly 80-hour workweek, (2) increasing the hourly wage calculated on the basis of a weekly 40-hour workweek, (3) and recognizing the union. It is expected that this major strike will break the record since the union was founded, and will effectively shut down the national textile industry. If this prediction becomes a reality, the economic situation in North Carolina, South Carolina, Georgia, and Massachusetts will come to a standstill, as more than half of the nation's textile factories are located in these four states. However, the factories also declared that 6,000 cotton workers in the New England area will oppose the strike, which shows that the general strike is not a unanimous action of all workers. (National Telegram on the 31st)

Shifts in the Japanese-Dutch Conference 93

Both Sides Show a Trend of Compromise

Batavia Special Dispatch: The Japanese-Dutch conference, which was once on the verge of collapse due to the Dutch East Indies government's promulgation of import restrictions on ceramics, has suddenly changed in recent days. The reason is that recently, Japanese Consul General Koshida and Dutch East Indies Deputy Minister of Economic Affairs Van Hoofstraaten, as well as Japanese chief representative Nagaoka and Dutch chief representative Meulenaf, have held several secret meetings. Both sides have shown a trend of compromise, so their opinions are gradually converging.

At this conference, the Dutch side originally intended to raise the discussion of maritime transport issues, but due to strong opposition from Tokyo, the Dutch side was extremely dissatisfied. Today, the Dutch side has already made concessions and agreed to raise it at the conference. Although this hurdle has not been resolved, it is clear that both sides have reached a considerable understanding. The so-called maritime transport issue refers to the cargo transport alliance between Java and Japan. In order to avoid fierce competition, the Japanese and Dutch shipping companies reached an agreement on July 10 last year by Nanyang Shipping, Osaka Merchant Shipping, Ishihara Steamship, and Java Shipping, and jointly abide by it. The content of the agreement is very simple, roughly as follows: (1) Navigation: The ships of each company shall not navigate between Java and Japan more than three times a month. (2) Freight: The same tonnage shall be used as a unit, and the freight rate shall be consistent. (3) Resolution: Important matters must be passed unanimously, and minor problems shall be decided by majority. (4) Reserve fund: A joint deposit of 25,000 yuan shall be made as a reserve fund. (5) Withdrawal: Withdrawal from this agreement must be notified three months in advance.

After the establishment of this agreement, the Dutch side discovered many shortcomings and was quite unfavorable to them, so they requested further discussion. In addition, the more important points of understanding between Japan and the Netherlands are: (1) The Dutch side should promise to give considerable consideration to the repeal of the import restriction order on ceramics. (2) In the future, the Dutch side should not impose restrictions on the import of other commodities at the conference.

Because of the above understandings, the future of the conference has shown a glimmer of hope. However, whether the Japanese-Dutch conference can go smoothly from now on, we still dare not be overly optimistic, and we will wait and see what happens.

Great Flood in the Dongjiang River in Guangdong Province 94

Dike Breaks for Over a Hundred Zhang in Shangdong Village, Dongguan

Huiyang Becomes a Waterland, Losses in the Millions

Guangzhou Dispatch: In recent months, the counties in the eastern region of Guangdong Province have been plagued by continuous rain. The Han River and Dongjiang River have caused disastrous floods. The counties along the river have all become waterlands. At the beginning of the month, Meixian County was flooded into the city, and Jiaoling County's suburbs continued to suffer from floods. By the end of this month, the floods from the upper reaches of the Dongjiang River converged and flowed down, so Dongguan, Boluo, Huiyang, and other counties in the lower reaches of the Dongjiang River were the first to bear the brunt. The dike in Shangdong Village, District 5, Dongguan County, suddenly collapsed on the 22nd. The dike base at Tanwen in the north of the village collapsed for over a hundred zhang. The houses, fields, livestock, and crops inside the dike were all submerged. Furniture and property were washed away, and thousands of villagers, supporting the old and leading the young, fled to the hills. It was truly an unprecedented disaster, and the losses of the entire village were no less than ten thousand yuan. At the moment, the refugees are eating in the wind and sleeping in the open, and the situation is miserable.

Huiyang County is located where the lower reaches of the Dongjiang River merge with the West River. The eastern flood suddenly rose more than five zhang on the 21st, and after the 21st, it rose nearly a foot every hour. Therefore, under the Bell Tower of Huizhou Prefecture City, Datiehang, Liujiaoting, Xiushui Lake, Ehu, Dashijie, North and South City, as well as the county city's Shuidong Road, Tiejinhu, Huangjiatang, Donggong Bridge, Ximenkou, and the Pubuchang and Tangxia Rice Street outside the city, were all vast and boundless. The water level was as high as the eaves, and the streets and alleys all depended on small boats for transportation. Those with buildings at home were all huddled in the attic, otherwise the whole family would be exposed to the high mounds. The entire city market has been suspended, peddlers have disappeared, and occasionally there are rafts transporting food to supply the refugees in the household. Unscrupulous merchants took the opportunity to manipulate the price, and each yuan of rice was one sheng more expensive. Other vegetables were several times more expensive than in the past. The highways from Hui to various counties, such as the Hui-Shan, Hui-Ping, Hui-Bo, Jia-Hui, and Hui-Dan roads, have been washed away by the water. Vehicles have been completely suspended since the 20th. The Hui-Zhang highway is related to the Guang-Jiu railway for joint transportation. The road company tried to use boats to ferry passengers through the flooded areas of the road to maintain transportation. As for telecommunications, due to the telegraph poles being knocked down by the flood, telecommunications were temporarily cut off, and mail was also suspended.

In the Rutengwen area of ​​Rubi Township, Huiyang County, the dike collapsed for dozens of feet, more than 30 houses collapsed, more than 100 acres of rice fields were destroyed, and more than 50 villagers drowned. The agricultural products in Sanduozhu and Pingshan and other places have been completely lost. The remaining low-lying villages along Huibo are all in the water. From a distance, only the tops of the trees can be seen. Refugees gather on the hills, crying for food. Judging from the disaster situation in Huiyang County alone, the loss should be more than one million yuan. In addition, the disaster situations in Boluo and Dongguan are no less than this. (August 26)

Jiangxi Bandits 95

Suffer a Crushing Defeat Attacking Xunwu County

A Puppet Customs Bureau is Smashed on the East Bank of the Gan River

Guangzhou Dispatch: On August 18, about 700 Jiangxi Eastern Red bandits from the 5th Independent Regiment of the puppet government, detoured from Huichang to attack Xunwu County. Fortunately, the 囗th Army's 囗th Division, which was stationed nearby, dispatched its subordinate troops to suppress them upon receiving the report. Later, the 囗囗 Battalion took the lead in attacking, and the 囗囗囗 Battalion outflanked them on different routes. The bandits stubbornly resisted on Danzhu Ping Hill. The 囗th Regiment 囗th Battalion used machine guns to strafe the bandit formation, and the 囗th Battalion outflanked the rear of the bandits, and the third battalion blocked the Red bandits' escape route to Qiannan. After a siege of several hours, more than 40 Red bandits were wounded and killed, and more than 90 were captured. The rest of the crowd began to collapse into the mountains. This was one of the battles in which the bandits of the Second Column were deeply wounded after Kejun Gate.

As for the First Column, in recent days, due to the prevalence of bandits in southern Hunan, various units have been ordered to step up their alert. When Xiao bandit harassed southeastern Hunan, more than 100 guerrillas of the puppet Xinkangxiong and Yu counties were suddenly discovered in Nankang County. The 囗th Army stationed in Dayu dispatched troops to surround the bandits on the highlands in the pit. The bandits resisted for about three hours and fled in panic. In this battle, the 囗 team killed more than 30 bandits, captured a puppet platoon attached Wang Xinglong, seized three Hubei-made single-barrel guns, and a large bundle of reactionary propaganda. On the 19th, the 囗th Division of the 囗th Army stationed in Gan County suddenly reported that Jiangkou Red bandits had set up a puppet customs office there. The 囗 division immediately dispatched troops to suppress them overnight, taking the route of Yangtang Dam and Liuhe. It was already about 3:00 in the morning. The bandits were awakened from their sleep and were caught off guard. They were surrounded and disarmed by the 囗 battalion. The remaining bandits fled in the water. When the puppet customs general bureau, the trade bureau, and the cooperative, and other puppet institutions were destroyed, a lot of supplies such as salt, cloth, rice, and oil were seized, as well as two to thirty million yuan of puppet banknotes, a horse, and two puppet cooperative wooden boats. Seven or eighty bandits were killed. It was found that Jiangkou is located on the east bank of the Gan River and borders Yudu, so the Red bandits set up a puppet tax collection agency in other places, and there was also a puppet district and township government and about 100 puppet first advance teams stationed there. Later, it was detected that there were about several hundred bandits ambushing in Datianwei, East Bank, and troops were sent to suppress them. After two hours of fighting, the Red bandits fled to Yudu, leaving behind more than ten guns. Since the Yudu bandits retreated, the 6th Independent Regiment of the puppet government in Huichang again invaded the defense area of ​​the 1st Division of Anyuan, Longbuwei. Yesterday, I received a telegram report from Yu Hanmou, the first army commander, which said, "Confidential, the bandit's puppet 6th Independent Regiment and guerrillas, a total of seven or eight hundred people, attacked on Ma Ri (21st) morning. Our troops fought fiercely with them for two hours, and the bandits fled to Caoziping, still trying to resist with danger. After our army pressed them, they collapsed to Shizizhai. In this battle, more than a hundred bandits were killed along the way, and more than thirty pseudo bandits were captured. Thirty-five rifles were seized. Two soldiers in our army were injured. Yu Hanmou bowed to the stem (23rd) seal" (August 25).

Continuous Rain in Gansu and Shaanxi 96

The Yellow River Water Level Rises Sharply

Li Yizhi Telegraphs the Executive Yuan for Instructions

Kaifeng Communication: The Yellow River Conservancy Commission received a report today that at 12:00 on the 28th in Shanzhou, the water level was 292.71 feet, and the flow rate was 3,200 cubic meters per second, which was about 3 centimeters lower than on the 27th. At 8:00 on the 28th at Qinchang, the water level was 94.06 meters, and the flow rate was about 7,000 cubic meters per second. At 12:00, the water level was 94.096 meters, and the flow was quite stable. However, from the 21st to the 26th in Lanzhou, the rain did not stop, and the Yellow River flow rate had reached 50 cubic meters per second. Recently, there has also been heavy rain in Shaanxi. The water potential in the upper reaches is huge, and the river defense of the three provinces will become more tense. In addition to telegraphing the governments of Hebei, Shandong, and Henan and the river affairs bureaus to prepare for emergencies, Li Yizhi telegraphed the Executive Yuan for instructions, saying, "According to reports, the rain has not stopped in Lanzhou from Ma (21st) to You (26th), and the river flow has reached 50 cubic meters per second. Recently, there has also been heavy rain in Shaanxi. If all the water flows to Tongguan at the same time, the downstream river defenses will be tight, and the old mouth of Changyuan, which has been breached and not blocked, will be irretrievable. We have telegraphed the governments of Hebei, Shandong, and Henan and the river affairs bureaus to prepare for emergencies. However, Hebei's flood control is particularly worrying due to the lack of funds and materials. If last year's floods are staged again, not only will the people suffer more, but the government's relief funds will also be spent more. I am worried and dare not remain silent. The time is pressing, and it seems that emergency measures should be taken. How should we handle this? Please give your instructions and I will obey them. Li Yizhi, Chairman of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, sincerely thanks you, seal."

(August 28)

Mongolian Political Committee 97

Political Affairs are Virtually at a Standstill

He Yingqin is Too Busy to Concurrently Serve as Director

Ping Dispatch: Yunduan Wangchuk, Chairman of the Mongolian Autonomous Political Committee, previously resigned from his position as League Leader and Zasak of Ulanqab League to the Mongolian-Tibetan Council, in order to dedicate himself to serving as a member of the Mongolian Political Committee. After being comforted by the Chairman of the Mongolian-Tibetan Council, Shi Qingyang, he has now withdrawn his resignation. However, due to funding problems, all political affairs of the Mongolian Political Committee have been virtually at a standstill recently. As for the Mongolian Guidance Director's Office, although the Mongolian people are extremely eager to establish it as soon as possible, Chairman He Yingqin is afraid that he will be unable to take care of it due to his busy official duties, so the official organization is still uncertain. Guo Wang and Bao Yueqing paid another visit to He on the 24th night to urge him. According to Guo Wang, "I and Bao Yueqing came to Ping to pay a visit to He to urge him to take office as the Inner Mongolia Autonomous Guidance Director. The report that I have left Ping and returned to Mongolia is inaccurate. It has not yet been determined when and where the Guidance Director's Office will be established. Chairman He Yingqin will not be able to go there in person when the office is established due to his busy military affairs. He will send a councilor of the Military Branch to participate. The results of our visit to He were extremely satisfactory." Also, Bao Yueqing said, "I and Guo Wang have visited Chairman He again. He will decide on the issue of whether or not to take office as the Guidance Director within a few days, and then reply to us. Recently, Prince De has often telegraphed me, urging me to persuade Chairman He to accept this position. We will return to Bailingmiao to report after the matter is completed. He has decided not to go there in person when the office is established."

According to sources concerned, Chairman He is unable to take care of the position of Mongolian Autonomous Guidance Director due to his busy official duties. This is a practical difficulty. However, the Mongolian people are extremely eager for He to take office to appease their longing. As for the location of the Guidance Director's Office, it has not yet been determined whether it will be located in Suiyuan or Bailingmiao, and the time has not been decided.

Serious Drought in Tongxiang, Zhejiang Province 98

Farmers Dig Ponds for Drinking Water, Wheat Bran for Food

Old Women Snatching Rice to Beg for Food is Often Heard

Tongxiang, Zhejiang, has not rained since the beginning of this summer, and the weather has been extremely hot, causing a severe drought. The river ports are dry, the land is cracked, and the farmland in the four townships lacks water for irrigation. Most of the crops have withered, and there is no hope for the autumn harvest. In particular, the Fuyuan in District 1 and the Tudian in District 4 have higher terrain, and the disaster is more severe. Only 30% of the early rice has been planted, and most of the people who have not sown are catching and transplanting seedlings, but due to lack of water for irrigation, they have all withered. Everywhere is a barren field, and secondary products such as tobacco, hemp, cypress, beans, melons, and fruits are scarce due to dry soil and lack of moisture. The livelihood of farmers has fallen into a state of hardship. Even relatively well-off families have to pawn their belongings to borrow rice, while ordinary poor households have already run out of food and have no way to borrow. They are extremely miserable. Villagers are digging ponds for drinking water and eating wheat bran to satisfy their hunger. The famine is getting worse, and the moans of the hungry are everywhere. In the past month, old women have come to the town to snatch rice to beg for food, which is often heard. The most severe storms are in Tudian, Shiwan, and other places. All the rivers in the town are now dry and the bottom can be seen. The daily drinking water for the citizens has caused panic. They all have to walk six or seven miles to Tanghe (the Grand Canal) to fetch water. The price of water has skyrocketed to several corners per load, which is still not enough. Every drop is precious. Navigation in all places has been stranded, and transportation is inconvenient. The price of rice is rising to about eleven yuan per day, and the people's food is worrying. The autumn heat has been very strong in recent days, and the humidity is uncomfortable. Moreover, due to unclean drinking water, epidemics are prevalent, and several deaths from epidemics are reported every day. The severity of the disaster is truly unparalleled. (Our correspondent Wu Wukang, August 29)

Songjiang 99

The Director of National Tax Collection is Sent to the Province

Ye Zongcheng, the first director of the National Tax Collection in this county, was dismissed from his position by the county government and placed under surveillance for alleged fraud in the collection of grain conversion and extra taxes. It has been almost a month. Local people Wu Boyang, Xu Shiqi, Zhang Huanzhi, and Zhu Zhaosheng, as well as fellow villagers abroad, have telegraphed the provincial government, stating that the national tax is related to the official supply and is of utmost importance. They requested that the provincial government investigate whether there is any inside story. The provincial government sent a commissioner to Songjiang to personally interrogate him. Ye Zongcheng confessed to everything, but the local people believed that there might be other circumstances. Wu Boyang, Wang Jieshi, Zhang Huanzhi, and other eight people went to the province together to visit Director Zhao and requested that he be brought to the province for strict interrogation to clarify the truth. Yesterday, the county government suddenly received a provincial order instructing them to send Ye Zongcheng to the province for verification. County Magistrate Jin sent staff member Wang Bangzhen to escort him to Shanghai in a car hired at 11:00 am on the 31st, and then take the train to the province to be sent to the Finance Department for disposal.

Suzhou 100

Extremely Serious Disaster in Dongting East Mountain

Yesterday, more than 1,000 farmers from 30 villages including Xiwu, Wangshe, and Shiqiao reported to the district office, saying that there had been no rain in Dongting East Mountain for three months, the river water was shallow and dry, and the paddy fields and aquatic products were hopeless. They requested that measures be taken to provide relief. Double Suicide of Male and Female Students 101

At the Mingli Inn in Yangshu Lane, outside Changmen, on the 29th, a young male and female traveler arrived, dressed in fashionable attire. They booked room number 19. The male was named Wang Yunqing, and the female, Hua Baolin, both aged sixteen. Around 6 PM on the 30th, a tea server saw the female putting a black substance into a hollow pill, which aroused suspicion. He also found a small amount of opium residue in the spittoon. He immediately reported this to the front desk, who then reported it to the relevant police precinct. Police arrived and sent the two to Suyong Hospital for examination. It was confirmed that they had taken poison. The male guest had taken too much poison and died around 9 PM that evening. The female guest had taken less and survived. The District Attorney's Office sent personnel for examination yesterday (31st) morning and ordered the family to prepare for the burial. According to the female guest, she was from Changzhou and had been living in Shanghai since the age of sixteen. She and the deceased, Wang Yunqing, were childhood sweethearts. Her father died when she was three, and she lived with her 35-year-old widowed mother. She had studied in Suzhou for two years and currently resided at No. 109 Daqing Lane, Great Eastern Road, Shanghai, at Mr. Chen Zegao's Shanghai residence. Over the years, she had been cared for by Mr. Chen. Wang Yunqing was a student at Gezhi Middle School in Shanghai. They had known each other for many years. Recently, as Wang grew older, he was attracted to the girl's graceful demeanor and pursued her, seeking a lifelong commitment. The girl refused because Wang's mother ran a brothel in Huile Lane. They had maintained a friendly relationship for two years. The day before, Wang Yunqing invited the girl to Suzhou to relieve his boredom. The girl couldn't bear to refuse and accompanied him. After arriving in Suzhou, Wang again asked the girl to marry him, but she still refused, maintaining only a friendly relationship. They talked all night and did not engage in physical intimacy. On the afternoon of the 30th, Wang, because the girl refused to marry him, took the opium he had brought from Shanghai, put it in a hollow pill, and swallowed it with wine. Seeing Wang taking poison, the girl felt ashamed to face her mother and also took poison, intending to die together. Wang lived at the dentist Jin Jiuru's place on Sanma Road in Shanghai and did not live with his mother. Wang's family arrived in Suzhou yesterday to handle all the arrangements.

Kunshan 102

Husband Hangs Himself Due to Wife's Affair

Zhao Er'a, a farmer from Lujiazhaiji outside the West Gate of this county, was by nature tyrannical and lecherous. Consequently, he had an affair with Mrs. Zhao, the wife of Chen Shuigen, a neighbor. Over time, the entire village knew about it, and Chen had also heard rumors. However, because of his cowardly nature, he could do nothing about it. Unexpectedly, yesterday, Zhao Er'a first severely beat his own wife and then incited his mistress, Mrs. Zhao, to quarrel with her husband in every way possible, declaring that she would no longer be Chen's wife. After the quarrel, Chen, in a moment of anger, went to a small room and hanged himself. After his family discovered him and cut him down, they tried to save him in every way possible, but it was too late to revive him.

Wuxi 103

Daylight Robbery by Thugs

At the home of the widowed Mrs. Zhu Miao, in Bo Du Port, outside the South Gate, around 11 AM the day before yesterday, four unknown men suddenly arrived. After entering, they closed the main gate and claimed they were searching for contraband. They barged into the inner room, overturning boxes and chests, searching extensively. Mrs. Miao assumed they were bandits and dared not make a sound. A neighbor, Mr. Jia, also heard the commotion and quickly reported it to the local watch post, which dispatched police to apprehend them. By the time the police arrived, the four men had already left. Subsequently, one person, Zou Tingliang, was apprehended in the fields behind the Xintai Rice Shop. Later, Zhou A'da and Zhang Er'a were apprehended in the alley of the Hengtai Rice Shop. They were all taken to the police station and handed over to the Public Security Bureau. Yesterday (31st), they were transferred to the local branch of the court along with Zhu Miao. After the prosecutor held a hearing, Zhu Miao was ordered to return home, and Zou Tingliang and the others were taken into custody.

Changshu 105

Rural Schools Effectively Shut Down

The education funds for this county, for the second half of last year, were only released for two and a half terms. From the 21st year to the present, there are as many as eleven terms in arrears. The bureau cannot clear the accounts, and the education sector is struggling to maintain operations. Now that Lu Jingmo has taken over as the director, it is even more impossible to raise funds. The schools have already started one after another, but there is no solution for the education fees, both old arrears and new installments. However, the schools are in great need of funds, so as of now, most rural schools have been unable to hold classes. As a result, some teachers jointly petitioned the bureau the day before yesterday for the release of funds, but to no avail. It is now known that the bureau has borrowed 37,000 yuan from the Jiangsu Farmers' Banks, but it needs the approval of the banks and the issuance of a payment order from the Department of Finance. In reality, it is still difficult, causing the rural education here to effectively shut down.

Changzhou 106

Cigarette Industry Opposes Increased Taxation

After Zhu Dagu, the newly appointed director of the Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Collection Office in Wuyi, took office, cigarette and alcohol merchants believed that the tax increase of five to ten times was difficult to bear and rose up in opposition. Yesterday (30th) at 12 PM, an emergency meeting was held at the Shuonan Guild Hall to discuss countermeasures. The result of the discussion was that the cigarette merchants in this county do not have branch companies or distribution points. What they sell is all wholesale in nature, so-called "whole buying and retail selling". According to the license tax regulations, they should not pay this heavy tax. At a time when rural areas are bankrupt and commerce is declining, merchants cannot bear this heavy burden. It was resolved that the original tax payment would be submitted by the Cigarette Industry Association to the County Chamber of Commerce and paid to the Tax Collection Office. At the same time, the Marketing Alcohol and Sauce Guild would jointly file a complaint with the provincial government, the Department of Finance, the Jiangsu Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Bureau, and the local Party and government authorities, alleging illegal and excessive taxation. The cigarette paper shops in the rural areas also requested the Cigarette Guild to find ways to provide relief.

Haimen 107

Pu Zhuping, the owner of the Central Pharmacy in the county and city, was found to be trafficking in drugs. On June 5th of this year, personnel from the Nantong District Security Command came to search, and they were caught red-handed. After repeated interrogations, he confessed without hesitation. He was sentenced to death in accordance with the Strict Prohibition of Highly Addictive Drugs Ordinance and submitted to the Nanchang Military Headquarters for approval. Yesterday (29th) morning at 8 AM, Judge Zhu from the District Command brought Pu out, verified his identity, and escorted him to Xiaoying outside the West Gate of Nantong for execution by firing squad. Upon hearing the news, the family immediately rushed to claim the body for burial.

Letter from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance 109

Dear Editor,

Having recently read in your newspaper a news item that the central government has approved Jiangsu Province's issuance of 20 million in public bonds to consolidate old debts and use the remaining funds to complete the Huai River Diversion Project, we find this to be inconsistent with the facts. We are providing a detailed list of the various uses for this public bond issuance: (1) 8 million for the construction of new canals; (2) 4 million for disaster relief and work relief in this province; (3) 6 million for Huai River diversion into the sea; (4) 2 million for the redemption of construction public bonds, totaling 20 million.

We are writing to request a correction.

Sincerely,

Secretariat of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance

August 30th

Local News

Transfer of Sichuan Grain to Regulate Drought in Jiangsu and Zhejiang 110

National Federation of Commerce Telegraphs Request for Exemption of Transit Taxes

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce of the Republic of China yesterday telegraphed the government authorities, Nanjing National Government Executive Yuan Ministry of Finance Ministry of Industry Ministry of Transportation Ministry of Railways Nanchang Chairman Jiang Junjian Jian:

We have received a telegram from the Chongqing Chamber of Commerce Zheng Ri Dian Wen. We believe that low grain prices hurt farmers, which is a natural phenomenon. If the collection of taxes is slightly relaxed, those who have grain will not rush to sell it, causing prices to fall further and farmers to be harmed. At a time when banditry has not been cleared and military needs are vast, the authorities' multiple tax levies a year are unavoidable. If the people's strength is not exhausted, they should endure the pain and transport it. However, it is like an empty house in nine out of ten cases, as if it has been completely emptied. In this situation, if the bandits are not quelled, the people cannot avoid death, and it is feared that even if the bandits are quelled, the people will die first. We should ask the authorities to use their soldiers and comfort the people in an inevitable situation, taking both sides into consideration, and temporarily postpone the pursuit of calls so that they can wait for prices.

Also, this year, the drought in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and other provinces has been severe. Reports say that several hundred thousand stones of foreign rice have been ordered. If Sichuan Province can unite with Hunan and Hubei to exempt all transit rice donations and order Sichuan River vessels to reduce transportation costs and lighten the cost, then the urgently needed rice in Jiangsu and Zhejiang will not have to be sought abroad, and the surplus rice in Sichuan Province can be used to dredge it, and the value will not be difficult to increase. The constant and immutable methods for adjusting the people's food supply are to purchase grain in abundant years and sell grain in lean years. The backward views have not been seen to be chosen. We humbly request your review and decision, and humbly request that you promptly order the two provinces of Sichuan and Hunan to resist foreign rice, on the one hand, and to circulate stored grain, on the other hand, which will benefit both national economy and people's livelihood. We pray that you will grant our request with utmost sincerity.

Chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce of the Republic of China, Lin Kanghou, printed.

Repeated Showers 111

Grain Prices Gradually Fall Back

Yesterday, Rice Dropped More Than Two Corners, Flour Dropped One Corner

In this city, after autumn, the drought has been long-lasting, and the heat has been severe, so food prices have soared. The Food Committee has resolved to restrict rice shops from hoarding and raising prices, with the highest price per dan not exceeding 13 yuan and 5 corners, and the price of each bag of flour has also risen by 3 to 4 corners. Since the sudden heavy showers on the 29th and 30th of last month, there has been standing water on the roads, and the weather has turned cooler. The rice markets in southern and northern Shanghai have also seen a pullback. Yesterday, rice prices fell back by two corners or more, and the price of each bag of flour also fell by about one corner. With the cloudy weather, there is a strong tendency for rain to continue, and people's hearts are gradually relaxing. Also, the Saigon rice that has been ordered will continue to arrive in Shanghai, so the price of rice in Shanghai is expected to continue to fall.

Yesterday Was the Birthday of the Queen of the Netherlands 113

Dutch Consulate Hosts Reception for Various Sectors

Mayor Wu and Others Attended to Offer Congratulations

Yesterday was the 54th birthday of Queen Wilhelmina of the Netherlands. All public and private Dutch institutions in this city flew the national flag and had a holiday to celebrate. The Dutch Consul General, Mr. Ge Longmen, hosted guests from various sectors in Shanghai at his residence, No. 5 Jia'er Yiai Road, in the French Concession from 11:30 AM to 12:30 PM. Many people attended, including Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Secretary Tang Shixuan, Section Chief Zhao Tiezhang, Secretary Zhang Mengling of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Shanghai Office, and consuls and military attaches from various countries, including Britain, France, the United States, Italy, Japan, and Germany. Mr. Ge personally hosted them and offered champagne, etc. They dispersed one after another at 12:30 PM. It is said that the Dutch community in this city, in addition to the Consul General hosting foreign guests, did not hold other celebrations because Prince Hendrik (the Queen's husband) had recently passed away.

Jiangsu Provincial Public Debt Distribution Uses 114

Completely Used for Construction

Opening New Canals, Diverting the Huai River into the Sea, and Disaster Relief

Establishment of a Bank Mortgage Supervision Committee

According to Xin Xin News Agency, the Jiangsu Provincial Government issued public bonds of 30 million yuan to develop water conservancy and consolidate old debts. Since the amount of public debt was approved by the central government and reduced to 20 million yuan, the uses have been re-stipulated to be completely used for construction and disaster relief in various counties of Jiangsu Province. The following is a record of the various circumstances ascertained by Xin Xin News Agency reporters:

Allocation of Uses 115

The Jiangsu Provincial Government issued the motive for this public bond, all for the consolidation of old debts, to carry out various constructions, and to relieve the disaster victims in the counties south of the Yangtze River. Its original allocated uses were (1) 6 million to return old debts and interest to various banks, (2) 9 million to redeem old public bonds at a price, (3) 6.5 million to open new canals, (4) 6.5 million to complete the Huai River diversion into the sea project, and (5) 2 million for the canal construction expenses in southern Jiangsu. Xin Xin News Agency reporters learned from the Jiangsu Bank yesterday that the provincial government has now reduced the amount of the public bond to 20 million, so the original distribution has been changed to (1) 8 million to open up new canals, (2) 6 million to the Huai River into the sea project, (4) 4 million to relieve the drought in various counties south of the Yangtze River, (4) 2 million to recover the Jiangsu Construction Public Bonds. As for repaying old debts, the amount is reduced, and it is not enough to distribute it, so it will be temporarily delayed.

Fund Guarantee 116

When Zhao Dihua, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Government Department of Finance, contacted the banking community, it was originally intended to use the 1.5 million yuan of salt tax allocated by the Ministry of Finance as a part of the fund. Now that the amount of public bonds has been reduced, the old debts cannot be repaid, so in order to maintain great faith, the salt tax money will be continuously consolidated. As for the fund for the new public bonds, it has now been decided to use the Jiangsu Construction Public Bond fund and the field and house deed tax from 60 counties in the province as a part of the fund. The remaining insufficient amount will be allocated from the field tax or another appropriate guarantee will be raised. It has not yet been decided.

Mortgage Cash 117

The banking community has stated that the new public bond has been stated to be completely used for construction and disaster relief, and will never be used for administrative expenses. In the future, it will be happy to assist in mortgaging loans to banks to promote its success. However, it is hoped that the use of the public bond must be in accordance with the planned distribution and completely used for construction. At the same time, it must not be forced to purchase from the people of Jiangsu or flow into the market. At the time, a use supervision committee must be organized to strictly supervise and show great faith.

Municipal Budget for the 23rd Year 118

Municipal Government Completes Compilation

Education Expenses Increase Annually

According to Central News Agency, the municipal budget for the 23rd year has been compiled by the municipal government and submitted to the municipal council for review. It will then be submitted to the central government for record. The following is a conversation with Zhu Fengwei, Section Chief of the Third Section of the Municipal Government:

Deficit in Last Year's Final Accounts 119

According to Zhu, last year's final accounts have been compiled and show a deficit of approximately 840,000 yuan. The reason is that the actual income last year did not reach the budgeted amount. The accumulated deficit over the years is approximately 3.42 million yuan. The deficit will be remedied in the future in various years.

No More Deficits This Year 120

As for this year's budget, all income and expenditure has been accurately estimated. The vehicle and vessel tax and house tax have been approved by the central government to appropriately increase the tax rate, so it is higher than last year's, with a total amount of 10.5 million. All administrative and career expenses of the various organs under the municipal government are distributed within this amount, so there may be no deficits this year.

Increased Education Funding 121

Education funding has been stipulated at 1.468 million yuan this year. The funding for each bureau has not increased this year, but education funding has increased annually, which shows that this city attaches great importance to education.

Liu Xiang 122

Hopes to Dismiss His Resignation

Sichuan People Telegraph the Central Government to Comfort and Retain Him

His representative in Shanghai, Deng Mingjie, took the 11 o'clock night express train to Beijing last night to prepare to meet with President Wang and, if necessary, go to Ganzhou to meet with Chairman Jiang to discuss everything. Before leaving, Deng told Far East News Agency reporters that although Commissioner Liu had not yet expressed his intention to continue to be responsible for bandit suppression and military affairs despite the persuasion of the central government, the generals in Sichuan, and various legal groups inside and outside Sichuan, he was still actively arranging for bandit suppression military affairs before the central government approved his resignation, and planned to go to the front line to command in the near future. The bandits are gathering at the junction of Wanyuan and Suixuan counties and are surrounded by the national army. The situation in Sichuan is now stable and has not been affected by Commissioner Liu's resignation.

Original Telegram of Presentation 123

According to Shen Shi News Agency, after Liu Xiang, Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression and Commissioner of Sichuan Rehabilitation, left Chengdu for Chongqing and telegraphed to the central government to resign from his concurrent posts, letters and telegrams were sent from all sides, earnestly persuading him to stay. Shen Shi News Agency reporters received an airmail letter from a friend in Chongqing yesterday saying that Liu's resignation was expected to be dismissed and that he had decided to depart to the front line to supervise the army and strive to complete the work of bandit suppression. The full text of Liu's telegram of resignation to the central government was also attached, as follows:

Chairman Lin of the Nanjing National Government, President Wang of the Executive Yuan, Chairman Jiang of Nanchang, Jian, and secret, Xiang was ordered to suppress the red, and it has been ten months. Thanks to Jun Zuo's virtue, the cities and towns lost in the north road were recovered in order. The bandits are poor and occupy Wanyuan, and have reached the final time of struggle. It is only because the steps of each road are not uniform, which makes the merits of nine rungs a failure. My five-way lone army advanced bravely, recklessly and died to attack strongly, and the losses were huge. At present, the dangerous suppression and control, I understand that there are no other concerns, but how to maintain it in the future is difficult to follow. Xiang Su is foolish and does not Shang Fu Xiao. If there is room for wandering, he will not be wronged to seek perfection. However, for a year, the brain and blood have been twisted, and the mind and strength have been exhausted. The micro-special is not helpful at this time, and the floating words outside the game are measured by the heart of unscrupulousness. If one corner is like this, the overall situation can be known. I expect that Jun Zuo will preside over the overall plan, and his difficulties must be hundreds of times more than Xiang. This is why Xiang wants to say it and stops, and dare not rashly Chen. However, the situation has reached this point, how can he bear to be silent? Although Sichuan is far away, it is very important to the overall situation. If the cotton strength is exhausted, it will be difficult in the coming days. The central government should relieve Xiang of his various positions and choose another capable person to plan his achievements and avoid falling. All the positions of Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression, Commissioner of Rehabilitation, and Commander of the 21st Army will be temporarily represented by the Chief of Staff from today. I am waiting for disposal, and I am compelled to speak, and I hope to see it.

Sichuan People Retain Him 124

According to the news from the Sichuan Shanghai Fellow Association, the elders of Sichuan, Zeng Jian, because the red force was rampant, and Liu Xiang, Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in Sichuan, suddenly felt that military affairs were thorny at the critical moment and resigned from his concurrent positions to the central government. The impact was very great, and the corruption was worrying. A special telegram was presented to the central government and the Sichuan Shanghai Fellow Association to unanimously retain him, so as to avoid the expansion of the bandit forces and the sinking of Shenzhou, and the upper and lower military and civilians will perish together.

Jiangsu Farmers' Two Banks 126

Decide on Cooperation Methods

Jiangsu Focuses on Assisting the Development of Industry and Commerce

Farmers Handle Disaster Relief and Other Matters in Rural Areas

According to Xin Xin News Agency, Tian Shitai, Association Director of Jiangsu Bank, said yesterday that the Jiangsu Bank and the Jiangsu Farmers' Bank have decided to cooperate separately on the issues of rural relief and industrial and commercial development after receiving orders from the Department of Finance to cooperate. The following is a record of the various situations:

Decide on Cooperation Methods 127

It is said that since the Jiangsu and Farmers' Banks received the order from the Department of Finance to discuss cooperation methods so that business could be further developed, the main personnel of the two banks held a joint meeting in Zhenjiang some time ago, and Qian agreed that the two banks belong to the province and should do their best to cooperate. It was decided that the Jiangsu Bank will specialize in investing in the development of industry and commerce, and the Jiangsu Farmers' Bank will specialize in handling rural relief matters, such as holding farmer loans, etc., so as to cooperate separately and develop business.

Both Banks' Businesses are Developed 128

The Jiangsu Provincial Treasury has always been managed by Jiangsu Bank, and the county treasury has also been managed by the bank since the 23rd year. The bank's business has been fairly developed in recent years, with 16 branches specializing in various industrial and commercial credit investments. The business of the Farmers' Bank is also not bad, and there are currently 26 branches and offices in various places.

Hebei Labor Dispute Resolved 129

Labor Leaders in Shanghai are Paid by the Company and Sent Back

Those Not in Shanghai Will Try to Contract for a Project

According to Guowen News Agency, more than 100 workers from Hebei traveled from Zhejiang to Anhui some time ago. After passing Dongjiadu Wharf, they were unwilling to move forward and went to the Provincial Shanghai Fellow Association to request relief. The association helped to negotiate with Fuyuan Company to pay their salaries because they belonged to the same hometown. At the same time, they requested the Public Security Bureau to provide relief. There were many misunderstandings during the period. The matter has now been largely resolved. All labor leaders who remain in the fellow association and are in Shanghai will be paid and sent back to their hometowns by the association. Those labor leaders who are not in Shanghai will not be paid for the time being, and the association will try to contract a project with the municipal government to maintain their livelihoods.

China Merchants Minsheng 130

River-Sea Intermodal Transport Implemented Today

Intermodal Transport Contract Officially Signed

Six-Month Trial Begins Today

China Merchants Bureau and Minsheng Shipping Company have agreed on river-sea intermodal transport in 21 major ports including the Sichuan River, the Yangtze River, the North and South, etc. First, 18 articles of the draft agreement were agreed upon, and then 28 articles of the detailed rules for intermodal transport were added. This information was published in this newspaper long ago. At present, the intermodal transport method has been formulated by both parties. China Merchants Bureau will not add any more river ships above Yichang in addition to the existing sailing ships. Minsheng Company will also not expand the Yihan, Xianghan, and Yangtze River routes. For all upstream cargo transported from the north and south and Shanghai to Sichuan and transferred to Minsheng ships, the bill of lading will be issued by China Merchants. For downstream cargo transported from Yu Yi, regardless of which port it is loaded to and transported by China Merchants ships, the bill of lading will be issued by Minsheng. The minimum bill of lading must be at least five yuan. As for the freight rates of both parties in the intermodal transport, they are also determined by route. Both parties provide convenience in the transportation, storage, and stacking of passenger and cargo within the scope of all routes. The detailed rules for intermodal transport were completed on the 30th of last month and the formal intermodal transport alliance was officially signed yesterday afternoon. From today (September 1), the 21-port cooperative intermodal transport of China Merchants Minsheng River-Sea will take effect. China Merchants Bureau immediately notified the branch offices to comply. As for the implementation period of the contract, it is first set for a six-month trial. If it is effective after the trial period, it will continue to be extended. If you do not want intermodal transport after the expiration, you can also cancel it.

Overseas Chinese Merchants Establish Xinghua National Products Company 131

Good Opportunity to Promote National Products in Nanyang

Overseas Chinese in Nanyang have always loved their motherland and have been enthusiastic about purchasing national products for a long time. Since Chen Gongbo of the Ministry of Industry went to Nanyang to investigate and announced the government's virtues, overseas Chinese have become more enthusiastic. Recently, a group of solid overseas Chinese merchants in Nanyang Singapore have jointly established Xinghua National Products Company, specializing in the promotion of national products. The capital is strong and the reputation is well-known. The Shanghai China National Products Production and Marketing Union is entrusted to purchase samples of goods for selection and promotion. All national industry and commerce countries are fortunate to send goods like them as soon as possible, so don't miss a good opportunity.

Hua Yang Relief Association 132

News on Continued Drought Disaster Relief Efforts

According to news from the Hua Yang Relief Association on Renji Road, they have recently received numerous letters and telegrams from various provinces requesting relief for the drought disaster. The disaster situation in Anhui, Jiangsu, and Zhejiang provinces has been briefly reported in this newspaper before. Now, we will continue to publish excerpts from letters from Henan, Jiangxi, Hubei, and other provinces, selecting the most significant ones: (1) Shangcheng County, Henan: According to the letter, there has been no rain for two months, the fields are cracked, drought-resistant crops have not been planted, and autumn crops have completely withered. It is estimated that the county produces 700,000 shi of rice and 300,000 shi of drought-resistant crops annually. At a price of ten yuan per shi, the income could exceed ten million yuan. Even if there is timely rain now, nine-tenths of the crops have already been damaged. If it is delayed for another ten days, even this remaining one-tenth will be completely lost. There are no grain reserves in the local area, and people's livelihoods are cut off. The future looks bleak and worrying. (2) Hukou County, Jiangxi: This county is located at the mouth of Poyang Lake, on the bank of the Yangtze River, with a small area. In years of good harvest, the grain is only enough to sustain for five months, and the rest is obtained from outside. Since the beginning of summer this year, there has been a severe drought with no rain, and irrigation has been cut off. Beans, cotton, rice, and sorghum have all withered and died. The affected farmland covers 170,000 mu, and the number of disaster-stricken households reaches over 24,000. People are panicked and desperately awaiting food. (3) Pengze County: This county is also a small county in Jiangxi, plagued by floods and droughts for years, and people's livelihoods are already difficult. This summer, there has been no rain for three months, ponds and weirs have dried up, cotton seedlings are short and stunted, and rice seedlings are yellow and scorched. Farmers are at a loss and their livelihoods are cut off. Currently, they can only look up at the empty sky, and innocent people will again suffer disaster. (4) Yuanjiang County, Hunan: Since midsummer, the county has been constantly sunny, resulting in calamities. The water sources have dried up, and there is no way to irrigate. The crops in the large fields have all withered, and the autumn harvest is hopeless. In addition, epidemics are prevalent, and deaths are occurring one after another. If no measures are taken to provide relief, the suffering of the residents is unpredictable. (5) Linxiang County: This county has been plagued by floods and droughts for years, and its vitality has been depleted for a long time. Between spring and summer this year, there was continuous rain, and seedlings were damaged, so three to four tenths could not be planted. After the beginning of summer, the drought demon raged, and there was no rain for a month. Weirs and ponds dried up, and crops turned completely red. There was no way to obtain drinking water. Under these circumstances, farmers have no choice but to stop farming, weep, and await death. (6) Shaoyang County: This county had little rain between spring and summer this year. Recently, the heat has intensified after autumn, and the fields have completely withered. There are no remnants of miscellaneous grains. This area, which has been impoverished by frequent droughts and barrenness, has again suffered this strange disaster. Farmers' livelihoods have reached a dead end. Selling wives and children is often heard of, and people are displaced and wander on the roads. If timely relief is not provided, those who are cunning and fierce will inevitably gather as bandits, which will affect public security and is truly chilling.

A Glimpse of the Attitude of Postal Workers

The Ministry of Communications convened a national postal conference, which opened in Beijing this morning. Cotton Merchants Association Telegram 139

Telegram from the Cotton Merchants Association to the Yuan, Ministry, and Commission: To the Legislative Yuan, Executive Yuan, Ministry of Industry, National Economic Commission, and Cotton Control Commission: We merchants previously stated that the promulgated regulations for cracking down on cotton are fraught with many obstacles. We intend to earnestly promote inspection first, and then implement the crackdown. We have telegraphed our situation on Yangri and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce has also telegraphed the matter. According to Article 14 of the crackdown regulations, the date of implementation of these regulations shall be determined by order. It is clear that it cannot take effect before it is announced. However, the Shanghai Chinese Cotton Mill Federation published a notice yesterday, implementing all the provisions of the regulations from September 1. This kind of illegal act cannot be recognized by us merchants. However, as the new cotton is about to be launched on the market, if no measures are taken to stop it, it will have a significant impact on market transactions. If disputes arise as a result, it will endanger the national cotton industry. In addition to immediately publishing a denial in the newspaper, we hereby telegraph the situation to your Yuan, Ministry, and Commission, requesting you to order a clear prohibition. On the one hand, the Ministry of Industry should promote inspection in advance, so as to improve it in an orderly manner and ensure the livelihood of the industry. At the end of the telegram, we await your urgent orders, The Shanghai Cotton Merchants Association, all merchants. Yan.

Red Pill King 140

Zhou Shengfa Handed Over to the Public Security Bureau Yesterday

Because This Case Is of Great Importance

Further Investigation Is Still Necessary

Zhou Shengfa, a native of Yuyao, known as the Red Pill King, recently raised huge funds to manufacture large-scale Hong Wan machines under the Flying Horse brand. He secretly transported them to other ports for sale, with distribution points in various ports, making huge profits. Countless people have been harmed. Up to now, it is said that Zhou owns more than one million gold dollars in ill-gotten gains, including movable and immovable property. This spring, 2.4 million red pills, worth more than 200,000 gold dollars, were seized at the North Railway Station. The criminals Zhao Zuting and Wang Weicheng (aka Little Wang), as well as three police officers who sheltered the red pills, were arrested and sent to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters for interrogation and executed by firing squad. According to Wang Weicheng's confession, the main culprit, Zhou Shengfa, has been wanted in Shanghai. Director Wen of the Public Security Bureau has paid special attention to this case and secretly ordered Captain Lu of the Criminal Investigation Team to select squad leader Ling Tianpeng to lead detectives to investigate and arrest him. After receiving the order, squad leader Ling remained calm and conducted a secret investigation. Later, he discovered that the suspect Zhou was hiding in house number 20, lane 707, Yuanyuanli, Gordon Road. He disguised himself and, together with Chinese and Western detectives, spent 57 days to capture Zhou Shengfa, the main culprit in the red pill poisoning case. He was handed over to the First Special District Court and transferred to the Nanshi District Court. The duty prosecutor, Lei Binzhang, proposed a trial and ordered him to be detained pending further instructions. This was reported in previous newspapers. Now it is learned that at 11 a.m. yesterday, Director Wen Hongen of the Public Security Bureau prepared a document and ordered squad leader Ling Tianpeng, detectives Zhang Zhenhai, Xu Changbiao, Lü Zhenliao, Gui Guofang, Yuan Shanlin, and others, who handled this case, to submit a request to the local court to transfer the suspect Zhou Shengfa back to the bureau for interrogation. Judge Zhang Zi presented it to President Shen Xiqing and Chief Prosecutor Lou Ying for approval. A preliminary hearing was opened, and Zhou Shengfa, who was in custody, was brought to the court. After a brief interrogation, the court ordered the officers to take him back to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation. It was found that the suspect Zhou was wearing a white short shirt and trousers, with a burly figure, exceptionally strong, full of smiles, and a calm demeanor. When the suspect was taken down from the court, he had a bag, but because his hands were handcuffed, it was inconvenient for him to carry it, so a detective carried it for him. Zhou repeatedly thanked him and strode out of the court, boarding a car (the Public Security Bureau's prisoner transport vehicle) awaiting instructions.

Seventh Term of Aviation Lottery Opened 141

Special Prize is Number 424462, Sold by the Mei Hua Li Watch Store, Aviation Highway Construction Lottery of the National Government, The seventh term of the lottery was opened yesterday afternoon in Yiyuan in public. were drawn first. At about 3 o'clock, the third prize, "296523", and "157931" were drawn. Then the second prize, "429469," and several third and fourth prizes were drawn. The Special Prize Was Difficult to Produce After all the prizes of all levels were drawn, Huang Guoen 147

reported that the first prize that had been drawn earlier had not been sold. According to the regulations, the special prize would be drawn separately. Hotel Industry Asks the Public Works Department 151

to Explain the Reason for the Tax Increase

Because the Tax Increase Points Published are Very Doubtful

The Tax Office Replied that a Reassessment Can Be Requested

According to Xinxin News Agency, the problem of the Public Works Department's increase in the hotel industry's room tax has not been resolved for two months. This time, the hotel industry has many doubts about the reasons for the tax increase sent by the Public Works Department. Now, a letter has been sent to the office to ask for an explanation. The reporter of Xinxin News Agency is now looking for and recording the correspondence between the hotel industry and the Tax Office, which is divided as follows:

Asking for an Explanation 152

Respectfully, at 10 a.m. on the 22nd of this month, the association sent representatives Sun Qiuping and others to meet with you to state the public opinion regarding your office's increase in room tax. I am grateful for your director's audience and for publishing the reasons for the tax increase. According to the reports of the representatives, there are many doubts about the points published by your director. Now I would like to list them as follows, hoping that you will reply so that I can tell the industry members: (1) Room tax is based on rent, which is the unchanging rule of the Ministry of Civil Affairs, and the amount of rent is based on contracts or rent receipts and old-fashioned vouchers, which is also the unchanging practice of the Public Works Department. Now your office uses the price of the room to estimate the tax, and the hotel industry uses the house and time as a commodity, and collects room tax, and uses the commodity to estimate, which is equivalent to using the commodity price as the standard for tax collection, which is a change of the original rules of the Public Works Department, which should be explained first. (2) The hotels that have been taxed this time are all considered by your director to be too cheap after the houses were built, so they must be re-evaluated now. The buildings of the hotels that have been taxed were all built four or five years or eight or nine years ago, when the land prices, material prices, and rents were all at the highest level. When the construction was completed, the Public Works Department had already admitted that the rents of both parties were in line with the valuation of the Public Works Department. Now, material prices are falling, and land and housing market prices are all affected. On the contrary, it is said that the estimates are too low, which should be explained second. (3) The hotels that have been taxed all have lease contracts to prove, but your director said that the lease period is very long, and there is no such thing as a long lease of 25 years, and there is no forgery in this. Before operating a hotel, it is necessary to obtain the consent of the landlord on the lease term, and the two parties sign a contract before starting business. The capital of a wild hotel is mostly in the decoration and property, if the landlord does not agree to the lease term, the entire property will be thrown into waste once the term is demolished. Anyone who knows a little about the hotel industry can say it. Furthermore, in long-term leases, the landlord and tenant have different views on whether the rent will rise or fall in the future. As a result, the initial rent will be higher than the normal rent, the middle period will be straight, and the end period will be lower. Anyone who is familiar with economic principles and social conditions can know it. As for whether it is forged, there should be proof, how can it be assumed? This should be explained third. Please explain the above three points immediately, and I will be very grateful. Sincerely to Mr. Bao En, Deputy Director of the Tax Office of the Public Works Department,

Reassessment 153

In reply, I received your letter on August 28, expressing deep dissatisfaction with the assessment of tax payment. I think that if you want to reassess, you may as well ask the Public Works Department's Tax Assessment Committee for it. The committee has a fair assessment of whether the price assessed by our office is fair. The application should be obtained from our office in person. Because of the previous letter, I hereby reply, hoping that you will check it. Sincerely to the Hotel Industry Association, Bao En,

Verdict in the One-Consort Case 160

Xie Peide and Hong Chengde Found Not Guilty

Part of the Hong Case Adjourned for Further Hearing

Xie Peide, business manager of Shanghai Cement Company, and Hong Chengde, a wealthy merchant, along with Hong's concubine, were recently sued by Madam Chen Wang, represented by lawyers Yen Yeh and Fu-Kang, for the murder of her daughter Chen Zhujun (also known as One-Consort Lao Liu). The Special Court has summoned them several times, but due to Hong Chengde's absence, the hearings have been repeatedly postponed, as reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon at 3:30, Judge Wu Zehan opened the second criminal court for questioning. Hong Chengde also surrendered himself. According to Hong's statement, on April 26th, Xie Peide called him and his concubine to Chen Zhujun's residence. Chen and Hong's concubine were friends. At the time, Chen wanted to move to Hong's house because she could no longer stay where she was, so they took Xie's car to Hong's place. That day, Chen made a phone call to Yang Binghu, saying that she was now at the Hong's residence and that they could discuss matters there. On the 28th, Yang and others came to Hong's house. Yang Binghu first apologized to Xie, then asked to speak with Chen in the bathroom privately. Chen then went into the bathroom with him. Less than ten minutes later, four gunshots were heard, and both of them were found dead in the bathroom. Subsequently, Ji Binkui, a Chinese detective from the Chengdu Road Police Station, testified that on April 28th, after receiving a report, he went with Western detective Cai Naitai to investigate. At the time, he saw Yang Binghu dead next to the bathroom door. There was a letter placed by the washbasin. He then saw a black jewelry box on the bed in the bedroom. Xie Peide was carrying it to another room. When he asked Xie whose it was, Xie replied that it was jewelry he had given to Chen Zhujun before. He then intervened, saying that since it had already been given as a gift, it belonged to her and could not be moved. After a brief inspection, he saw that the box was full of valuable jewelry such as diamond rings, bracelets, and diamond pendants, about twenty pieces in total, and a bank passbook in Chen Zhujun's name with a balance of one thousand yuan. He could not remember the name of the bank. There was also a divorce agreement, which Xie said he had given to Chen. The incident took place at the Sun Apartment, No. 561 Weihaiwei Road, which was under the jurisdiction of the Jing'an Temple Police Station, so the Western detective telegraphed the Jing'an Temple Police Station, and Chinese detective He Yunpu and Western detective Hua Sheng came. He then handed the jewelry box to detective He, and at that time, the divorce agreement had been hidden by Xie in his suit pocket. Subsequently, Western detective Cai Naitai testified, confirming that he had seen a black jewelry box, but only knew it contained jewelry and did not inspect the number of items. The rest of his testimony was similar to that of detective Ji. Yang Qiusun then testified about the circumstances at the time and presented a suicide note, which Yang Binghu had placed on the washbasin in the bathroom before his death. Lawyer Yen Yeh then asked Yang Qiusun if he had brought the threatening letter he had received. Yang replied that he had given it to the prosecutor during the autopsy. Lawyer Yen then asked him to announce the contents. Yang said that the letter generally said something like, "You have no son, only this one grandson. Now Yang Binghu is taking Xie Peide's love, and if you do not advise him, there will be harm to the grandfather and grandson." After hearing this, the court, with the facts clear, ordered the start of the debate. After the lawyers on both sides debated, Judge Wu declared the debate concluded and delivered the verdict in court. The main text of the verdict stated that Xie Peide and Hong Chengde were not guilty. The plaintiff's civil suit was dismissed. Part of the Hong case was adjourned for further hearing.
