Mayor Wu's Rectification 162

Time Limit for Applying for Land Measurement and Certificate Renewal

Three Months from Measurement to Signature of the Drawing

Mayor Wu of this city believes that the land occupancy certificate is the only proof of land ownership for the people. To facilitate the people, he recently ordered the Land Bureau to report the time limit for applying for land measurement and certificate renewal to the Municipal Government. The Municipal Government ordered the Land Bureau to set a time limit of three months from the dispatch of personnel for measurement to the signature of the drawing by the owner, and three months from the endorsement of the guarantor to the drawing and issuance of the certificate, except for cases where disputes arise. In total, six months is the maximum limit. Ordinary cases can be appropriately shortened, but not to less than three months, to show seriousness. In addition, three points are supplemented, and the Land Bureau is still ordered to properly draft improvement measures and submit them for approval. The three supplementary points are as follows: (1) For all land measurement and certificate renewal cases, before the scheduled measurement, the land guarantor should be ordered to report the four neighbors of the land, so that the neighbors can be notified at the same time to avoid disputes after the event. (2) If there are property disputes such as encroachment or unclear boundaries in the land to be measured, the Land Bureau should immediately stop the process or return the original documents to maintain the original state and have the court handle it. It should not be disposed of rashly. After the judgment is finalized, the process should be resumed. If there are cases such as applying for land measurement and transfer of contract due to incomplete evidence or other disputes, the original documents can also be returned to clarify responsibilities. (3) For the people's application for land measurement and certificate renewal, the Land Bureau has always only dispatched a surveyor from the Third Section for measurement, and the personnel in charge of the section do not participate. Relying only on the surveyor's report, and often scheduling measurements repeatedly, but failing to implement the measurement for years, is prone to corruption. The Land Bureau should find ways to change this and pay attention to it at any time to improve efficiency. As for the owner's deliberate evasion or self-delay, which causes the suspension and exceeds the time limit, the responsibility lies with the owner and not with the government, so there is no reason to criticize. The original procedure and time limit proposed by the Land Bureau are excerpted below. For the sake of speed, appropriate changes are made. When an owner applies for land measurement, he only needs to collect the property evidence, send it to the Fourth Section of the Bureau to issue a receipt, check the single grain tax, and order the payment of measurement fees at the same time, and schedule the measurement. The length of the measurement period depends on the number of cases and is arranged in order. That is, after the measurement date is scheduled, it may be delayed due to rain, the owner's absence, the debtor's avoidance of the field, or temporary disputes, resulting in postponement and rescheduling. After the surveyor completes the measurement, it must be processed, the measurement records must be sorted out, detailed drawings must be made, and the boundaries, area, drawings, examination, photography, review, drawing, and other procedures must be calculated. Moreover, these procedures are all interconnected and have their own difficulties. Therefore, if the land is free from encroachment disputes or other unclear procedures, it is estimated that the owner can be ordered to sign the drawings within three months. (The procedure is often interrupted at this point. If the owner receives the drawings and does not sign and send them immediately, or claims that the drawings are wrong and requests correction, it is often after a long time that they accuse the Bureau of being slow to process and make false accusations. This situation is not uncommon. If there is excess land, the Tax Section must be notified, but most owners often ignore the Bureau's notification of the Tax Section. The Tax Section's problem is not resolved, so the certificate cannot be made, which also causes delays.) After the drawings are signed and sent to the Bureau, the land guarantor is ordered to endorse them. (If the land guarantor is delayed in arriving, the Bureau will formulate other processing methods.) Within one and a half months after the endorsement, a topographic map of the household land will be drawn, and within one month, the land occupancy certificate will be filled out and sent. Within half a month after the certificate is made, the seal will be affixed and sealed, and various procedures such as affixing the hard seal and proofreading will be completed. In summary, the processing of land measurement cases takes three months from the completion of the measurement to ordering the signature of the drawings, and three months from the submission of the signed drawings to the issuance of the certificate. However, if there are disputes in the middle, it is difficult to predict the processing time limit. The reason why the various procedures after signing and submitting the drawings take three months is that the original intention of setting the time limit was to allow for a certain amount of time to be processed in order due to the increased workload, and to allow the neighboring households of the land to be measured an opportunity to object in order to be cautious and prevent problems. Now, it is planned to maintain this point and not change it.

Eight Yuan Rent Causes Trouble 163

Woman Beaten and Miscarries, Dies Tragically

Yu Zhang Causes a Major Disaster Out of Nothing

Xu Chen Injured and Miscarries, Dies in Vain

Xu Chen, a woman from Yangzhou, was 24 years old and lived at No. 237 Hong'an Lane, Haining Road. Her husband, Xu Wanyuan, was a cook with a meager income, so their finances were not very comfortable. They owed the sub-landlord Zhou Hongxu eight yuan in rent. Unexpectedly, on the 8th of last month, Yu Zhang, a woman living in the same house, suddenly falsely told Xu Chen that if she did not pay the rent, Zhou would evict them. Upon hearing this, Ms. Xu became suspicious and asked Zhou's younger sister, Yuezhi, for clarification, only to find out that it was not true. Therefore, at 1:00 PM that day, the two women quarreled with each other, and then engaged in a physical altercation. People intervened to stop them. However, Xu Chen was six months pregnant, and after being beaten, she felt excruciating abdominal pain. By 6:00 AM the next morning, the abdominal pain worsened, and she suddenly began to bleed. Her husband was extremely alarmed and rushed her to the Shanghai Nursing Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective. She died at 0:16 AM yesterday morning. The hospital reported this to the Hongkou Police Station, which ordered detective Jin Guanya to investigate. However, Yu Zhang had already fled without a trace several days earlier. The detective then transported the body to the autopsy room on Feilun Road. At around 10:00 AM, Guo Wei, a prosecutor from the First Special District Court, along with forensic doctor Zhang Yan and clerk Wang Zuyi, arrived at the scene to examine the body. According to the briefing by the Western police chief, and then according to Zhou Hongxu's statement, Zhou Hongxu, age 21, from Ningbo, who is a cook, is the sub-landlord of the house. The deceased lived on the third floor, and Yu Zhang lived in the pavilion room. On the day of the fight, he was out working, so he did not witness it. However, according to his sister, they had kicked each other. After his sister and neighbors intervened, they stopped. The deceased then felt abdominal pain. According to the deceased's husband, Xu Wanyuan, age 29, he owed the sub-landlord eight yuan in rent. Yu Zhang, who lived in the same house, suddenly told his wife that if they did not pay the sub-landlord, he would evict them. After questioning the sub-landlord's younger sister, they said that it was not true, so they knew that Yu was lying. At around 1:00 PM that day, he had gone out to work, and the two women suddenly quarreled with each other. When he returned home, his wife told him, and she said that she had been experiencing severe abdominal pain since then, and the next morning she miscarried. He then sent her to the hospital. Guo, upon receiving the statement, believed that Yu Zhang was indeed suspected of committing a crime and ordered the police station to strictly arrest her for investigation. He then ruled that the deceased, Xu Chen, female, died due to miscarriage. The body was handed over to her husband, Xu Wanyuan, to collect and bury.

China Travel Service 164

Organizes a Qiantang River Tide Watching Tour

As autumn arrives, the tides of Zhejiang will once again surge towards the sky. Chinese and Western visitors are flocking to the roads, all eager to witness the spectacular tides. Haining and Bapu are both excellent places to watch the tides, but Bapu is especially so. Bapu is located twenty miles east, where the riverbank juts out, and the surging tides rush in, encountering a sudden impact. One wave is blocked, while the other is not, meeting at Bapu, causing the tides to surge and crash like ten thousand galloping horses. It is truly a spectacle. The tides then turn into a curved line and rush towards Haining, so the high tides at Haining are only the rebound of the aftershocks from Bapu. Based on its experience, the China Travel Service in this city has scheduled special Bapu tide-watching tours on September 25th and 26th, limited to eighty people each day. Departures from Shanghai will be by special bus, with round-trip tickets costing ten yuan per person, including a lunch box meal. If traveling in groups of four, the bus can be dispatched to pick you up at your residence. Detailed regulations are available for review. Since this trip reaches Bapu via the Shanghai-Hangzhou highway, the scenery along the way is beautiful, and driving and sightseeing is even more enjoyable. Ladies and gentlemen who wish to watch the tides should book and purchase tickets as soon as possible to avoid disappointment.

City Chamber of Commerce Holds 166

Meeting to Study Industrial and Commercial Laws and Regulations

Determines the Candidates and Procedures for Group Research

Elected Fang Jiaobo and Li Wenjie as Standing Committee Members

The Industrial and Commercial Laws and Regulations Research Committee of the City Chamber of Commerce held its second meeting yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM. The following committee members attended: Wang Xiaowen, Fang Jiaobo, Lu Jun, Zhang Zhengxue, Yu Chengxiu, Sun Xiaolou, Wang Xiaotong, Jiang Wanping, Xi Yushu, Li Wenjie, Xu Yongzuo (representing Zhang Zhengxue), Xie Chunpu, and Pan Xulun (representing Li Wenjie), a total of thirteen people. First, the convener Li Wenjie reported on the establishment and expansion of the committee's organization. Then, Xi Yushu was elected as chairman and Li Wenjie as secretary. (A) Matters Reported: (1) Regarding the resolution of the previous meeting to suggest that the City Chamber of Commerce hire eight additional committee members, this has been done. The current committee has fifteen members, including eight lawyers and seven accountants. (2) Regarding the resolution of the previous meeting to request the City Chamber of Commerce to send letters to the members of various trade associations and store members, informing them that if any of the members have questions about industrial and commercial laws and regulations after the establishment of the committee, they can send letters to the committee for research and response, this has been done. (3) Regarding the resolution of the previous meeting to request the City Chamber of Commerce to petition the Legislative Yuan to allow the committee to receive the drafts of industrial and commercial laws and regulations before they are submitted for discussion, so that the committee can conduct detailed research with the relevant trade associations and contribute opinions for consideration, the Secretariat of the Legislative Yuan has replied, approving the referral to the Commercial Law Committee for reference. (B) Matters Discussed: (1) Regarding how the committee should be divided into research groups, it was resolved to divide into two groups: Commercial Law and Industrial Law. Wang Xiaowen, Wang Xiaotong, Zhang Zhengxue, Yu Chengxiu, Xi Yushu, Jiang Wanping, Fang Jiaobo, Guo Shouyi, and Lu Jun were elected to the Commercial Law Group; Sun Xiaolou, Pan Xulun, Xu Yongzuo, Cao Zhigong, and Li Wenjie were elected to the Industrial Law Group. (2) Regarding how the research procedures of the committee should be determined, it was resolved that the committee should elect two standing committee members to handle the allocation of research work. Afterwards, the committee will research industrial and commercial laws and regulations by means of correspondence and separate research. The standing committee members will recommend members of the commercial and industrial groups to take turns or jointly take responsibility. The recommended members will report the research results to the standing committee members within a certain period, who will forward them to the standing committee of the City Chamber of Commerce. If the standing committee deems it necessary, it may convene a plenary meeting of the committee for discussion and decision. (3) Regarding how the standing committee members should be elected, it was resolved to elect Fang Jiaobo and Li Wenjie as standing committee members to facilitate contact with the City Chamber of Commerce. (4) Regarding how the compilation and printing of the Industrial and Commercial Laws and Regulations Compilation, which was resolved at the previous meeting, should proceed, it was resolved to elect Wang Xiaowen, Zhang Zhengxue, Yu Chengxiu, Fang Jiaobo, Xu Yongzuo, Wang Xiaotong, and Li Wenjie for compilation, with Wang Xiaowen convening. (5) Regarding how the committee should express its opinions to the newly established Trademark Laws and Regulations Research Committee of the City Chamber of Commerce if it has opinions on amending trademark laws and regulations, it was resolved to send a letter to the City Chamber of Commerce, stating that if the committee has any questions, the committee is willing to participate and provide opinions. (6) Regarding whether the committee should appoint members to study the issue of [illegible characters], it was resolved to appoint Zhang Zhengxue, Yu Chengxiu, Xu Yongzuo, Xi Yushu, and Jiang Wanping for research, with Jiang Wanping convening. (7) Regarding the suggestion that the City Chamber of Commerce forward a request to the Legislative Yuan to send the drafting Insurance Law, Commercial Registration Law, and the currently being revised Negotiable Instruments Law and Savings Bank Law to the committee for research, the resolution was passed.

Minutes of the Executive Board Meeting of the Roads Association 169

Wu Shan Resigns, Fan Guang Still Acts as Director-General

Representative Office in Nanyang Ceases Activities

The Executive Board of the China National Roads Construction Association held a meeting yesterday. The following directors attended: Wu Tiecheng (represented by Li Dachao), Li Zhaohuan, Yin Ru　, Wu Kaisheng, Li Denghui, Yang Nianzu, Zhu Shaoping (represented by Wu Deyin), and Fan Guang. Until a successor is found, Director Fan Guang will be asked to diligently serve as acting director-general. The chairman expressed his deep gratitude for Director Fan Guang's efforts to improve the association's affairs, fully fulfill his obligations, and work selflessly during the past few months, as well as the special cost savings in office expenses. He also expressed his appreciation for the diligent service of the staff in all departments. (5) The chairman proposed that former Director-General Wu had worked diligently and effectively for more than ten years. Although he has resigned due to illness, the association should still seek his assistance in supporting the association's affairs. It was resolved to recommend Yin Ruyao, Wu Kaisheng, and Li Dachao to draft measures to allow Wu to demonstrate his strengths and submit them for discussion at the next meeting. (6) The representative office in Nanyang has not been well managed. How should it be handled? It was resolved to temporarily suspend the activities of the office and reconsider the matter after the organizational outline of the branch is revised. (7) The textbook "Bridge Engineering" has been sold out. Should it be reprinted? It was resolved to reprint. (Rest omitted)

Hai Ning Tidal News 172

The Qiantang River tide, commonly thought to be at its peak in mid-August, actually sees large tides almost every day after autumn begins. When strong winds blow, it becomes even more spectacular. This year, the Beijing-Shanghai, Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo railway authorities determined the largest tides would occur on August 27th, 28th, 29th, September 11th, 12th, 26th, 27th, and the 6th, and therefore, special round-trip tickets and bus tickets were sold for tide watching on these days. Passengers could take the train from Shanghai to Chang'an Station, transfer to a bus, and go directly to the Hai Ning riverside. The railway bureau built a tide-watching platform, allowing visitors to enter and take a seat with their tickets. August 27th was the first day the railway bureau sold tide-watching tickets. It was reported that Liu Dingxin, the deputy director of the railway bureau's traffic department, along with staff from various departments, went to inspect the arrangements. At that time, there were nearly a hundred visitors. The train left North Station at 7:55 AM and arrived at Chang'an Station after 11:00 AM. Many chartered long-distance buses were already waiting at the station, carrying the tourists directly to the banks of the Hai Ning River. They arrived at the destination in about half an hour. At that time, the tide had not yet arrived. The tourists strolled along the riverbank before entering the tide-watching platform. After about fifteen minutes, a line of white waves could be seen rising from the mouth of Hangzhou Bay, gradually extending. The sound of the tide rumbled like the sudden unfolding of spring thunder, shaking the distant sky. The white line grew longer and higher, and the rumble became deafening. When the white line connected in all directions and pushed forward, the raging waves surged, like ten thousand horses galloping. The viewers held their breath. The tide head was about seven feet high, rolling forward. Starting from 12:50 PM, the tide reached the Hai Ning riverside at 1:20 PM. The low-lying dikes along the coast were instantly submerged, and the remaining waves surged, still threatening to sweep ashore. It is said that yesterday the weather was hot. If it had been cloudy, rainy, or windy, the tide would have been even higher. The railway bureau's tide-watching platform was located to the right of the tide-watching pavilion on the riverbank, with comfortable facilities and drinks available for purchase. It was also reported that the railway bureau had arranged for a restaurant to prepare meals for the visitors to eat by the river. After the tide watching was completed that day, the tourists took buses back to Chang'an and boarded the 3:07 PM express train back to Shanghai.

Tobacco Exchange Industry Association 173

Request to Reduce License Tax

Notice to Members to Submit Reasons Individually

The Municipal Finance Bureau has been responsible for collecting the city's tobacco and alcohol license tax for two months. Director Cai's intention is to align with the regulations of the Ministry and rectify and collect the tax fairly. However, tobacco and alcohol merchants claim that "rectification" is simply a euphemism for raising taxes, which has already been implemented with increases ranging from one to several times. The fact that taxes have been increased is already evident, leading to widespread resentment. After the industry petitioned, they were met with understanding, and many were still charged the original amount of two or four yuan. However, the investigation by the tax collection office, due to a lack of understanding of the industry's intricacies, resulted in many unjust increases. According to the person in charge of the Tobacco Exchange Industry Association, many small shops with limited capital find it difficult to make a profit due to the small scale of their business and are unable to bear the increased tax burden. They have asked the association for help. The association has already selectively returned taxes to those who have applied, and for those who have been asked to pay more but have not yet done so, they request that the taxes be waived to show compassion and maintain livelihoods. Based on this, the association petitioned the Municipal Chamber of Commerce on August 29th to discuss relief measures. Members have already been notified to submit their reasons in writing from August 30th to September 5th, so that a roster can be compiled and sent to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to implore the authorities to handle the case together and request correction and reduction. It is reported that after the association issued the notice, several businesses, including Datianxiang on Tianbao Road, Lu Jintai on Ninghe Road, Baoyu on Dongjiadu, and Eryuanxing and Chen Ji on Houjia Road, have already registered. The association's notice is recorded below:

Notice regarding the petition to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce on the 29th of this month, with the following measures: (1) The autumn license tax donated by fellow businesses has increased from two yuan to four, eight, twelve, or twenty yuan. Various members have sent letters stating that their business is small-scale and profit margins are thin, making it difficult to earn a profit. Donating one yuan to maintain a livelihood is already challenging. How can they bear a multiple increase in taxes? A reduction or exemption is requested. (2) For households that have been subject to increased taxes, a roster has already been submitted to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to argue the case with the authorities. For households that have not yet been investigated, they should first inquire with the Municipal South Tax Collection Office to determine if the tax will be increased. If they are able to bear the increase, there is no need to argue. For those who are unable to bear the burden, please submit a written explanation of the reasons to this association within one week so that a supplementary roster can be compiled and sent to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to be forwarded to the Finance Bureau, requesting compassionate reduction. (3) If the authorities are unable to understand the situation, they will only be able to act in accordance with the resolutions of the joint meeting of tobacco and alcohol industry representatives. (Please pay attention to the above three items.) Members are requested to submit their reasons for being unable to bear the burden to this association from August 30th to September 5th, so that it can be reported to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to implore the authorities to grant a reduction. Please do not delay and cause harm. This notice is issued.

French Concession 175

Western Detective Agency Plans to Arrest Red Pill Traffickers

Wang Shousong, a Criminal in Distribution, Was Apprehended

Tracking Down the Leader Zou Agou

Drug King Zou Agou (from Suzhou) specializes in selling red pills and white powder (i.e., morphine and heroin contained in cigarette butts) and other drugs in the area of Ruifuli on Zilaihuo Street in the French Concession. He has dispatched dozens of accomplices (divided into day and night shifts) to trade in the streets and alleys, with very meticulous sales procedures. There are always more than 20 people on standby as lookouts, cashiers, token distributors, and goods distributors, patrolling the area. The mechanism for hiding the goods is very secret, even insiders do not know. The wholesale depot is located at No. 66 Ruifuli, but there are no drugs in the house, so although the police have heard of it, it is not easy to crack the case. Yesterday (i.e., the 31st) at 10:00 AM, the Western detective of the French Concession specializing in drug investigation led the Chinese detectives of the same team and drove in a truck to rush into No. 66 to search for and arrest the criminals. However, these people escaped through the back door in full force without any gains. At 3:00 PM in the afternoon, the Western detective secretly went to ambush with only two Chinese detectives, and finally apprehended Wang Shousong, a key criminal in distribution, with dozens of packets of red pills, morphine, heroin, and other drugs found on him. The rest escaped. He was taken into the police station along with the loot, and is currently tracking down the leader, drug king Zou Agou, to investigate and punish him according to the law in order to stop the drug scourge.

Fire Starter Chen Yang

Total of Fifteen Rooms Destroyed

At 0:20 PM yesterday afternoon, in the Shilimeyao area of ​​Xiaoshadu in western Shanghai, a fire broke out in the thatched cottage where Chen Yang, a woman from Anhui, lived, due to careless cooking and leaving fire and accumulated firewood. Results of the Re-trial of the Kidnapping Case after Appeal 178

Zheng Shifan's Sentence Reduced to Nine Years

Zhang Ashu's Appeal Was Rejected

Four years ago, Pu Wenjiang, the manager of Fuxin Flour Factory from Wuxi, and Qian Zhaofu, a local resident who runs the Yongfeng Wood Company in Nanshi, Shanghai, were kidnapped one after another in the French Concession. In the autumn of the year before last, the Chinese and Western detectives of the special organ of the French police arrested the gang of local criminals Zheng Shifan, Zhang Afu, and Zhang Jiancheng from Ningbo, and sent them to the Second Special Court. Zheng was sentenced to life imprisonment, and the two Zhangs were each sentenced to 20 years of imprisonment. Zhang Jiancheng was sentenced to death by the First Special Court for committing a kidnapping case in the Public Concession, and was executed. Later, Zheng and Zhang Afu refused to accept the judgment and appealed to the Third Branch of the High Court. As a result, Zheng Shifan's sentence was changed to 12 years of imprisonment, and Zhang Afu's sentence was changed to life imprisonment. The two criminals still refused to accept and filed a third instance appeal with the Supreme Court. After the Supreme Court reviewed the entire case file, it found that there were still doubts in the case, revoked the original judgment, and sent the case back to the Third Branch of the High Court for trial. The Third Branch of the High Court had investigated the witnesses and concluded the collegial panel trial, and announced that the judgment was awaiting a fixed date. The matter has been recorded in the newspaper. Yesterday was the date of the judgment. At 9:00 AM, Guo Dezhang, the chief of the criminal court, together with the two judges Sun and Fan and the prosecutor Zhang, specially opened the Third Criminal Court and ordered the two criminals Zheng and Zhang to be brought to court. The judgment revoked the part of the original judgment concerning Zheng Shifan's crime and punishment. Zheng Shifan was sentenced to nine years of imprisonment for assisting in kidnapping for ransom. The number of days of detention before the judgment was confirmed was calculated as two days equivalent to one day of imprisonment. Zhang Afu's appeal was rejected. After the judgment, the two criminals were still sent back to the detention center to await instructions.

Zhao Xilin Case 179

Suspect Ren Haoming Not Guilty

Zhao Xilin from Changzhou served as a detective in the local Public Security Bureau. After resigning, he came to Shanghai and was hired by Shenxin No. 9 Yarn Factory in Yangshupu as an inspector. At 6:45 AM on August 20th of the 20th year of the Republic of China, he was shot and knocked down by an enemy near the factory, attempting to harm his life. He was later sent to the hospital for treatment and recovered. In June of the following year, he was assassinated for the second time in the same way, shot and killed. Shen Yuzhou, the head of the Chinese detectives of Yangshupu Police Station, arrested the criminals Fang Renzhao, Wu Fafang, and Tang Bingchang and sent them to the First Special District Court. As a result, Fang and Wu were sentenced to life imprisonment, and Tang was sentenced to 15 years of imprisonment. It was found that an accomplice, Ren Haoming from Changzhou, was at large. He was recently arrested by detectives from the Putuo Road Police Station and sent to the court for interrogation. Because the location of the incident and the finalized criminals were handled by the Yangshupu Police Station, the police station still interrogated and supplied the details, which have been recorded in this newspaper. The case has been concluded and is awaiting judgment. Yesterday morning, Judge Wu Zehan went to the Third Criminal Court to announce the judgment that Ren Haoming was not guilty. The testimony of the family members of the victim in this case was contradictory and lacked sufficient evidence. Li Zhishan, the lawyer of the Public Works Department, requested that he be returned to custody during the appeal period, which was approved by the court.

Old Mother Lamented Poverty 180

Female Worker Committed Suicide by Drowning

Gong Xu, a woman from Jiangbei living at No. 53, Garbage Pond, North of Yangjiadu, Pudong, has a daughter named Genmei, 19 years old, who has been betrothed to someone but has not yet married. She is currently a female worker at the nearby Yingchang Match Factory. The mother and daughter have always been harmonious. After dinner at 8:00 PM the night before, they talked about the family's life. The mother was very anxious because her income could not cover her expenses, and she blamed Genmei for only making 27 or 28 chips per shift, saying that the wages she turned in were too low to make a living. Genmei was angry and frustrated because it was due to the slow work and not her lack of productivity. The old mother should not have blamed her too much. She pretended to go to Puxi with her sisters to watch a play. At night, she went to the riverbank and committed suicide by drowning, unbeknownst to her mother. Because no one noticed, she sacrificed her life. Her body floated to the surface of the Huangpu River at the Jinheyuan Wharf in the 16th Pu at about 10:00 AM yesterday morning. Two Chinese detectives, No. 15 and No. 93, of the Customs Water Patrol Police Station happened to see it and fished it out of the police station. While waiting for the Lifeboat Bureau to take it away for burial, the deceased's mother suddenly cried to the police station, claiming that she had not seen her daughter return all night and suspected that something had happened. Later, she heard a boatman report that she had died tragically in the river and requested that the body be claimed. The police station approved it.

For the well-being of its members, the association has established an ophthalmology department starting from September 1st. It has hired Dr. Zhang Zaishan, a former doctor from the Shibata Ophthalmology Hospital in Japan, as the director. The service hours are from 12 PM to 2 PM daily. All members, regardless of their membership type, can enjoy free preferential treatment. It is noted that eye and dental diseases are prevalent in the city. The association's preferential rates for dental and eye protection for members are quite advantageous. However, non-members will be charged one yuan for consultation.

Letter to the Editor 192

To the Editor: According to our client, Bei Shunrong, the report "Woman Injured in Stall Dispute" published in the newspaper on the 28th of this month contains inaccuracies. Ling A'da previously operated meat stall No. 63 in the Pingliang Road vegetable market. Upon A'da's death, and after failing to renew the license for three months, the Municipal Council's health department revoked the license, reclaimed the stall, and granted it to Shunrong for business. However, Zhu, the wife of Ling A'da, became enraged upon seeing Shunrong operating the stall and fabricated a story claiming that she entrusted Shunrong to manage the stall during her husband's illness, and that Shunrong then changed the name of Ling A'da without authorization. This is a complete fabrication and an attempt to mislead the public. Furthermore, she has repeatedly harassed him and intentionally cut her left arm with a knife in an attempt to frame him. There are witnesses to this. Instead of repenting, she further fabricates stories and publishes them in the newspaper, and attempts to use malicious influence to pressure the Municipal Council to revoke its decision and reinstate the old arrangement. Her methods are despicable. In addition to initiating criminal proceedings, we request that you publish this letter in your "Letters to the Editor" column to set the record straight. Accordingly, we respectfully request your consideration. Sincerely, Gu Jirong, Lawyer, addressed to the Shenbao Newspaper.

Reading Q & A 195

The Issue of Women's Self-Study After Marriage

| Reply to Liu Xunyue |

Reading Guidance:

Several years ago, I read Ni Huanzhi, written by Ye Shaojun. In the book, Ni Huanzhi's wife was initially a very promising teacher, but after marriage, she forgot her responsibilities and became a good wife and loving mother. Although the author eventually opened up a path for her, the change was abrupt. Why do women forget their responsibilities after marriage? How can we make her understand her responsibilities again and rescue her from the sea of suffering | which she considers happiness |?

Women, almost every woman buries her future after marriage. Their only hope is to raise children and carry on the family line. Their only duty is to serve their husbands, and they don't care about anything else. They never want to improve themselves again. This is not an exaggeration; I have seen many examples with my own eyes. I have a friend whose wife, as far as I know, was a smart and ambitious woman before marriage. But after marriage, when my friend gave her elementary social science books to read, she looked contentedly at the child beside her and smiled, "Why do we need to read these?" She sometimes reads novels, but only for entertainment. There is also my cousin's wife, who is even stranger. She is a graduate of a prestigious high school, and her grades were among the best in school. But after graduation, she got married, and now her daily routine, besides eating and sleeping, is just playing mahjong, watching movies, and indulging in neurotic, hysterical daydreams. She never reads books. Even popular novels like those from the Saturday Evening Post, or loud Peking opera, she cannot understand or find interesting. My cousin, who studies literature, originally wanted to marry a woman with a background in literature | or at least someone who didn't dislike literature | to study and learn together. But now, he is accompanied by a woman who is like a blind person. No, a blind person is even more independent. She is always afraid that her husband will harm his health by studying too hard, and she nags him constantly. I don't understand why she has become like this? How can I make her understand? How can I help her study on her own? I hope you can give me an answer. | Liu Xunyue

The question raised by Mr. Liu is indeed an interesting one, and it is also very meaningful because it is related to the entire society, the entire women's issue.

Since the May Fourth Movement shouted the first cry for liberation of Chinese women, although a small minority have already walked out of their boudoirs and into schools, even this small minority is only limited to entering schools and cannot take another step into society. As Mr. Liu's example shows, even the most promising woman in school is finished after marriage. This phenomenon is still very, very common today. It's not just a few individuals; almost all knowledgeable women are in danger of falling into this fate. Ni Huanzhi is a representative work depicting the youth of the era around the May Fourth Movement, so the book says that Ni Huanzhi's wife cannot escape the stereotypes of this era. The transformation after Ni Huanzhi's death is just a little inspiration that the author gives to new women.

Therefore, people in society have become skeptical about the liberation of women, believing that women are basically parasites who are willing to give up on themselves and do not seek independence and liberation. Their reading is only for vanity, their knowledge is just a decoration, and they use it to gain the title of a modern woman to show that they are different from old-fashioned women. Therefore, they can associate with noble people, fall in love, and eventually marry a noble husband. This is their only hope in life.

Germany Actively Preparing 198

Recent News from the World Olympic Games

Afghanistan Has Registered to Participate Zeppelin Airship Broadcasts to South America

(Berlin Communication) The 11th World Olympic Games will be held in Berlin in 1936. Germany is sparing no effort in its preparations. The Berlin Olympic Stadium is being constructed day and night and will be completed soon. The recent news is recorded as follows:

Afghanistan Registers to Participate 199

The Secretariat of the Games has received a notice from the Honorary Secretary of the Olympic Committee of the Kingdom of Afghanistan, registering to participate in the 11th World Olympic Games. Afghanistan will send a hockey team and a track and field team. Afghanistan is a mountainous country, standing on the Pamir Plateau, bordered by Persia to the west and Russian Turkestan to the north. The first West Asian Olympic Games, sponsored by the World Olympic Committee, were held in New Delhi on March 2nd and 3rd. India won the most, followed by Ceylon. In the hockey competition, India only beat Afghanistan 5-0. India can beat any European team, but can only beat Afghanistan 5-0. The strength of Afghanistan's hockey team is evident.

Zeppelin Airship Broadcasts 200

In ancient times, Greece sent trumpeters all over the country to call for participation in the Olympic Games. The last Los Angeles Games followed this idea, using a crowned trumpeter to call for global participation as the official logo of the Games. For the Berlin Games, Germany has selected a "bell" as the emblem of the Games. In addition, the Games will use the Zeppelin airship as a "caller" to invite South American countries to participate in Germany. The ship has contacted the radio station in the capital of Chile. Any new messages sent to the ship by the Organizing Committee will be broadcast to South American countries by radio as the ship crosses the Atlantic Ocean, greatly exciting listeners. The difference between ancient and modern propaganda methods is evident.

Reduce Travel Costs to Germany 201

The Organizing Committee has reached an agreement with the country's land and sea travel industry. Personnel and athletes of the national delegations participating in the Games who travel on ships and trains of German companies will receive special discounts. There are several routes: North Atlantic Route, South American West Coast Route, South American East Coast Route, East Asian and Australian Route, Cuban-Mexican Route, African Route, North American Route, South Pacific and Central American Route, and East Asian Route. There are set discounts for travel and freight costs.

Protect the Olympic Emblem Decree 202

Given the noble significance of the World Olympic Games, the emblems and logos of the Olympic Games must not be used for commercial or industrial advertising. The Games officially announced on June 28th of this year that anyone who has not obtained the official written permission of the Games may not use the bell-shaped emblem of the Games for commercial advertising. The same applies to individuals and companies. In order to respect the Games, it is hoped that other countries in the world will also have the same clear decree to protect the emblem of the Games.

In the Autumn Rain 203

A Record of the Sino-Japanese Tennis Players' Exhibition

Zheng Zhaojia Performed Exceptionally Well, Losing to Fujikura 3-6

Qiu Feihai Rushed Around, Losing to Yamagishi 1-6

Yamagishi and other Japanese players who attended the Davis Cup returned to their country via Shanghai. Yesterday, at 12:30 PM, they were invited to the Shanghai Lawn Tennis Club for an exhibition match. Approximately 700-800 people of various races came to watch, creating a lively atmosphere. Unfortunately, autumn rain fell during the match, diminishing its appeal. However, the spectators were happy to receive the rain after a long drought, and they were reluctant to leave despite getting wet. The competition was divided into two singles and two doubles matches, all of which were won by the Japanese players. However, Zheng Zhaojia's performance was unexpectedly wonderful, and he engaged in intense competition with the young Fujikura, ultimately losing 3-6. In the singles match between Qiu Feihai and Yamagishi, the situation was one-sided. Yamagishi showed his skills, and Qiu Feihai was unable to defend himself, resulting in a 6-1 defeat for Qiu. Yamagishi did not expend much effort. In the first doubles match, Fujikura and Nishimura played against Carlsen and Pennie Vieussen, but the match was not very exciting, with the Japanese players winning 6-4, 6-2. In the other doubles match, originally scheduled to be De Vau and Qiu Feihai, De Vau was late, so Carlsen and Qiu teamed up against Yamagishi and Nishimura. The rain became heavier after the first set, greatly reducing the interest. The result was also a 6-4, 6-2 victory for the Japanese players. The details are recorded below:

Yamagishi 204

Is the main player in the Davis Cup. He previously only played doubles, teaming up with Shizumura as a long-term partner. They are not only famous in the Far East but also enjoy a good reputation in Europe. Anyone familiar with tennis is likely to know Yamagishi and Shizumura. At the 9th Far Eastern Games held in Tokyo, Yamagishi and Sato Jiro, who committed suicide this year, were the singles representatives. Qiu Feihai fought against Yamagishi, but Qiu was exhausted and withdrew. Yamagishi has also performed in Tianjin and has participated in the Davis Cup three or four times. This year, due to Sato's suicide, he was promoted to the first singles representative, but was eliminated by Australia in the second week in Europe (4-1). At the Wimbledon Championships, Yamagishi was eliminated in the fourth week. Watching yesterday's performance, his true skills were rarely seen. His forehand and backhand shots were equally good, and the force of the shots was like arrows leaving the bow. Very few shots fell into the net or went out of bounds. When he had an opportunity, he was sure to win, hitting left and right, either deep into the baseline or close to the net, making it impossible for his opponent to defend. Qiu Feihai was manipulated and at a loss. His serve was also very powerful, and his high-pressure volleys at the net were excellent.

Fujikura 205

The young Fujikura is a graduate of Meiji University. In 1930, the Meiji University tennis team came to Shanghai for a competition, and people in Shanghai saw his style. He was only 19 years old, and his older brother was 20 years old when he passed away last year. At that time, the young Fujikura was still a novice, unable to withstand a single blow from Lin Qiu. But today, three years later, Fujikura is far from what he used to be, and he is causing a stir. In the Davis Cup, he defeated Australia's McGrath, achieving the only victory. His style of play is similar to Yamagishi's. His shots are beautiful, both forehand and backhand are good, he has a lot of experience, and his own errors are very rare. Young and handsome, he is a great tennis player of the future.

Nishimura 206

He is a doubles player. In terms of doubles play, Fujikura seems to be inferior to him. His high-pressure shots are excellent, and his net play is also good. His face resembles Han Langen in the Fishermen's Song. At first, it doesn't seem like it, but looking closely, it's quite similar, and the more you look, the more similar it is.

Singles 207

Zheng Zhaojia and Fujikura started first. Both were young and had the same style of play, but Zheng's skills were not as deep, and he made many errors. Fujikura won four games in a row easily. Seeing that the situation was not good, Zheng boldly used his strength, and with his courage strengthened, his movements became smoother. He swept left and right, the shots were sharp and quick, and they happened to pass over the net. Fujikura imitated him, and his shots were also extremely swift. Both of them displayed their strengths, which was very entertaining and earned a lot of applause from the audience. Seeing the fierce attack, Fujikura tried to go to the net, but it was useless. Zheng won three games in a row, but lost his serve in the next game, and his momentum waned. Fujikura won 6-3. Next was Qiu Feihai against Yamagishi. Qiu tried his best to fight, but his opponent's shots were too strong. One shot came from the left, and another came from the right, and Qiu could not defend himself. 6-1, Qiu suffered a crushing defeat, taking very little time.

Doubles 208

After the singles matches, there were doubles matches. Fujikura and Nishimura played against Carlsen and Pennie Vieussen. It was drizzling constantly, the ground was slippery, and the ball was wet. Neither side played with much spirit, especially Carlsen and Pennie Vieussen, whose movements were poor, and they touched the net and hit the ball out of bounds a lot. There was a brief fight in the first set, and each side won with their serve. After Carlsen's serve failed, they lost 4-6. In the second set, they lost again 2-6. In the next doubles match, because the long-legged De Vau was late, Carlsen and Qiu teamed up to fight against Yamagishi and Nishimura. The interest was very good. Yamagishi and Nishimura's lobs never went out of bounds, and they landed right in front of the baseline, two or three feet away. Their high-pressure shots could cross the net at the baseline like cannonballs, no less than a 128-caliber cannon. At first, each side won with their serve, but after Carlsen lost his serve in the fifth game, they lost 4-6. At that time, the rain became heavier, and it was thought that the match would be stopped, but Qiu's enthusiasm was not diminished, and they had to continue the match. The wet clothes and shoes were not a concern. The new tennis rackets that the Japanese players had specially made in England were a real pity. In the lackluster match, Yamagishi and Nishimura won again 6-2, and the competition ended. The Japanese players are scheduled to return to Japan tomorrow morning.

Education News

Improving Education Issues 213

Jiang and Wang Agree on Three Points

(Nanjing, 31st) It is reported that Wang Shijie's visit to Guling to discuss education issues with Chairman Chiang consisted of three points: (1) Chiang paid close attention to the use and management of the Kang funds and required efforts to improve them in the future. (2) Strictly assess the education authorities of each province and city and conduct strict assessments. (3) Promote the industrialization of education.

Development of Soviet Education 214

(TASS, Moscow, August 1st Dispatch) The implementation of compulsory education in the Soviet Union is progressing exceptionally rapidly. At the end of 1933, the total number of students in schools was 21,813,400, which is almost three times more than in the period before the revolution, from 1914 to 1915. Mass education outside of schools, such as adult literacy classes, is also being promoted on a large scale. The most important aspect in implementing universal education is the industrialization of schools, which aims to bridge the gap between physical and mental labor. Many schools have been established in factories, and machine tractor stations, state-owned and collective farms have also established their own schools. The organization of labor productivity is closely related to theoretical education. The following figures show the development of education after the October Revolution (student numbers in thousands):

Year Total number of primary and secondary schools Number of primary school students Number of secondary school students Total number of students

1914-15 106.400 7,113.6 564.6 7,800.6

1920-21 118.396 9,206.8 574.4 9,781.2

1928-29 124.429 10,468.4 1,606.4 12,074.8

1930-31 152.654 15,609.1 2,047.1 17,656.2

1932-33 167.254 18,179.4 3,634.0 21,813.4

The table shows that at the end of 1933, the number of primary school students increased by 251.2 percent compared to the period 1914-15, while the number of secondary school students increased by 643.6 percent. It is said that in 1934, the total number of students in various educational institutions in the Soviet Union will reach 24.2 million.

Chinese Economic Society 215

Eleventh Annual Meeting Minutes

The papers presented were all explorations of controlled economy

Next annual meeting to be held in Sichuan, Guangdong, or Guangxi

Zhou Zuomin, Pan Xulun, and Wang Zhixin elected as directors Changsha Special Dispatch: The opening ceremony of the 11th annual meeting of the Chinese Economic Society was held at Hunan University at Yuelu Mountain, Changsha, on August 26th. Papers were read all day on the 27th, and a banquet was held at the headquarters of the Western Route Bandit Suppression Army that evening. On the morning of the 28th, a board meeting was held to re-elect directors. The details are recorded below:

Reading of Papers 216

Attending Members: The venue for the paper reading session was still held in the Hunan University Library. It started at 9:00 AM on the 27th. Over eighty members were present, including Ma Yinchu, Li Quanshi, Tang Qingzeng, Xu Zhaosun, Liang Hancao, Chen Changheng, Wang Yuxiang, Dong Qizheng, Pan Moqing, Zhou Ren, Zhang Yuanjie, Zhuang Zhihuan, Jin Guobao, Pan Xulun, He Fengshan, Xu Jikang, Zhang Jingou, etc. Over one hundred guests were present as audience, including Zhu Jingnong, Director of the Hunan Education Department, Zhang Kailian, Director of the Finance Department, Yu Jichuan, Director of the Construction Department, Hu Shuhua, President of Hunan University, and students from the university's Department of Political Economy.

Chairman's Report: Tang Qingzeng, Chairman of the Annual Meeting Paper Committee, reported that the Paper Committee received a total of twenty papers. After review, they can be divided into two groups: the first group belongs to the obstacles of control, and the second group belongs to the methods of various controls. Half of the members were absent due to various reasons, so only half of the papers were read and discussed. Also, for the sake of saving time, each paper reading was limited to twenty minutes, with a bell warning at fifteen minutes. Discussions were also limited to twenty minutes. As usual, the audience could not speak, etc.

Reading of Papers: Eighteen papers were read: (1) "On the Monetary Revolution to Save the Nation" (Liu Ziren), (2) "Discussion on the Implementation of Controlled Economic Policies in China" (Ge Yufu), (3) "Discussion on the Steps of Implementing Economic Control" (Zhuang Zhihuan), (4) "The Economy that the Government Should Control" (Li Quanshi), (5) "The Problem of Remedying China's Foreign Trade Import Surplus" (Ma Yinchu), (6) "The Three Principles of the People and Controlled Economy" (Chen Changheng), (7) "Discussion on the Capacity Standard System", (8) "Controlled Planning Technology", (9) "Problems of Highway Transportation Control" (the above three papers are all by Wu Depei), (10) "The Cotton Industry Problem in China's Economic Control" (Deng Zhibing), (11) "Basic Construction of Controlled Economy" (He Youzao, Cai Guanmin), (12) "Scope of Controlling China's Foreign Trade" (Liu Tingmian), (13) "The Problem of Controlling China's Food" (Du Bangji), (14) "Economic Control and China's Salt Industry Financial Problems" (Jiang Qizhou), (15) "Problems of Controlling Foreign Trade" (Jia Shiyi), (16) "Controlled Economy and China's Shipping Industry", (17) "Discussion on Accounting Fraud Prevention", (18) "Communication Problems between Chinese and Western Accounting" (Li Yunliang). Only the papers of Liu Ziren, Zhuang Zhihuan, Li Quanshi, Ge Yufu, Chen Changheng, and Wu Depei were discussed. Ma Yinchu's paper was not presented because other members had also mentioned it. The others were absent. The full text of the papers will not be published for the time being and will be published in the quarterly journal by the editorial board of the society. After the discussion of the papers, Yu Jichuan and Zhang Kailian, the directors of Hunan's finance and construction departments, reported in detail on Hunan's past and recent construction and financial status. Finally, various issues concerning the production and sales of rice in Hunan Province were discussed. The meeting adjourned at around 6 o'clock. They then went to Jingyitang in the First Academy of Hunan University to attend a banquet hosted by He Jian, Commander-in-Chief of the Western Route Bandit Suppression Army.

Shen Bao Wireless Weekly

Test Oscillator 227

— Li Yuanqing

With a commonly used three-tube radio featuring single-stage regenerative detection and two-stage low-frequency amplification, only a multimeter and two batteries are needed to perform most repairs. However, this is not so easy with multi-stage tuned radio frequency or superheterodyne radios.

In general, the better the sensitivity and the better the selectivity of a radio, the more tuning circuits it has. The most complex radios today use variable capacitors with six or more gangs, and tuning circuits with more than ten stages. We know that the various stages of a radio must resonate with the incoming radio waves to achieve maximum efficiency. Therefore, radios using coaxial tuning must be absolutely synchronized at every stage, regardless of position. In other words, at any degree, the inductance and capacitance of each stage must be exactly equal to each other.

Of course, these radios have already undergone several extremely precise calibrations by the manufacturer before being sold. However, long-distance transport, prolonged use, or even a slight jolt can cause the various tuning circuits to lose their balance. Sometimes, even replacing a new vacuum tube can cause significant changes. Once the circuits are out of balance, it will not only significantly affect the sensitivity and selectivity of the radio, but also reduce the output volume and hinder clear sound quality.

Usually, to calibrate out-of-balance tuning circuits, one would first try to receive a broadcast from a distant station, and then adjust the trimming capacitors of each stage until the maximum sound level is achieved. This method of calibration is actually very difficult to be accurate. Because the human ear is not very sensitive to small changes in sound level (see "Ratio of Power to Volume" by this author in issue 43), and the strength of the radio waves coming from afar varies from time to time, it is indeed very difficult to obtain a satisfactory result.

From this point of view, it is best to have a small-scale signal generator of your own in order to cope with the situation with ease and not be at a loss. The so-called test oscillator is designed to meet this need.

The figure shows the simplest self-modulated test oscillator. The amount of amplitude modulation frequency varies with the amount of grid leak and grid capacitor. For the coil L, wind eighty turns of No. 22 double-stranded cotton-covered wire on a two-and-a-half-inch diameter cylinder, and tap a center line at forty turns. (See figure.) C is a 0.00035 mfd variable capacitor for adjusting the frequency. CI is a Io_mmf small variable capacitor for transmitting radio waves. The values of the other components are all detailed in the figure, so I will not repeat them here. (When using, connect end A to the antenna terminal of the receiving radio, and end G to the ground terminal.)

In order to save space, this article only briefly describes the need for and construction of a test oscillator. As for its usage and the calibration method for multi-stage tuning radios, I will write about it in detail later.

Filament Circuit Connection Method 228

— Ming Xiang

When using vacuum tubes, the filament voltage must be absolutely accurate. Because the filament structure is fragile, if it exceeds its specified value, the filament will generate a large amount of current, suddenly increasing its temperature. This can cause the filament to emit excessive electrons, reducing the life of the vacuum tube, or even cause the filament to burn out immediately and be destroyed in an instant. Therefore, when designing a radio, do not neglect the filament circuit because it is relatively simple. Beginners should be especially careful, otherwise they will suffer great losses.

The number of vacuum tubes in a radio is not limited to one, and the voltage and current of each one are not necessarily the same, so the problem is more complicated. Usually, the connection of filament circuits is nothing more than the following three methods:

Method 1: Connect the filaments of each vacuum tube in parallel and then connect them to the power supply. If the power supply voltage is too high and does not match, a resistor R can be connected in series to reduce it to the appropriate value. The only condition for using this method is that the filament voltage of each tube must be exactly the same. As shown in Figure 1, the value of R can be calculated using the formula:

LE is the power supply voltage, E1 is the filament voltage,

Figure 1 Figure 2 Figure 3 229

I1 I2 I3 is the filament current of each tube. For example, Figure 1 shows the parallel filament circuit of three vacuum tubes numbered 32, 30, and 33. The filament current of each tube is 0.06, 0.06, and 0.26 amps, and the voltage is 2 volts for all. The power supply is provided by two series-connected dry cells with a voltage of 3 volts. The value of R calculated according to the formula is Z.8 ohms.

Method 2: Connect the filaments of each tube in series and then connect them to the power supply. The power supply voltage should be equal to the sum of the voltages of each tube. If it is too high, a resistor R can also be connected in series to reduce it. The only condition for using this method is that the filament current of each tube must be exactly the same. As shown in Figure 2, the formula for calculating the value of R is:

E is the power supply voltage, E1 E2 E3 are the filament voltages of each tube, I is the current. For example, the filament circuit of the popular transformerless AC radio on the market uses this method. Now suppose a four-tube radio with vacuum tube models 3936, 38, and 25Z5. The filament voltage of 25Z5 is 25 volts, and the others are 6.3 volts. The filament current is the same at 0.3 amps. If connected in series and plugged directly into a 110V AC power supply, a resistor R must be added. According to the formula, it should be 220 ohms.

Method 3: This is also a parallel connection, similar to the first method, but it is used to compensate for different voltages of each tube. Vacuum tubes with lower filament voltages must be connected to a separate resistor R1 to reduce it, as shown in Figure 3. The calculation formula is:

E1 is the voltage at the common parallel connection, is the filament voltage of the E2 vacuum tube, I1 is its current. For example, in Figure 3, two tubes are No. 201 and one is No. 22. The voltage at E1 is the filament voltage of 201, which is 5 volts. E2 is the filament voltage of 22, which needs 3.3 volts. The filament current I1 is 0.132 amps (these numbers can be found on the vacuum tube characteristics table). The value of R1 calculated according to the formula should be 13 ohms.

The choice of the above three methods depends on the vacuum tubes used in the radio. If the filament voltages of each vacuum tube are exactly the same, the first method can be used. If the filament currents are the same, the second method can be used. If the voltage and current are different, then the third method should be used.

Ultra-Long Wave Transmitter 230

— Chen Kexiao

Now in the radio world, everyone is moving towards ultra-short waves; but the author is running towards long waves. Isn't this reversing the course of radio? That's right. The disadvantage of long waves is that they consume a lot of power and their effectiveness is far less than that of short waves. But this ultra-long wave transmitter is an exception. Because it consumes very little power, and its transmitting effectiveness is not bad, because the frequency is close to low frequency, the receiving end equipment does not need a detector to hear the radio signal. Therefore, it is necessary to introduce it to amateur comrades. It's just that the author has not yet made a long-distance communication test with this transmitter, so I can only ask all amateurs to help with the test. The circuit of this ultra-long wave transmitter is shown in the left figure. V can use 30 or 201 vacuum tubes. If 27A or 47A is used, the range will be even farther, but the B voltage must be increased. T is an ordinary low-frequency transformer, one to three, or one to five. C, the capacitance is forty-six trillionths of a farad, or thirty-five trillionths of a farad. The depletion resistor R that controls the filament voltage, and the A voltage must be determined according to the vacuum tube used. K is the telegraph key. The size of the B voltage must be determined according to the communication distance. Within a large 1/2 mile, the B voltage must be 22 1/2 V. Within four or five miles, the B voltage is probably between 45 volts and 90 volts. The most important device in the whole machine is the ground wire, so the ground wire is best made of an iron bar about four or five feet long. Drive it into the near-wet soil, leaving about two inches of the iron bar above the ground, and then tightly wrap the iron bar with a piece of copper skin, and then weld the skin wire of the ground wire firmly with tin. The antenna type can be any type, but the cage type is the best. If the communication distance is short, the receiving end only needs to connect the earpiece directly to the heaven and earth lines (that is, connect the earpiece in series in the heaven and earth lines) to receive the signal. If you use a vacuum tube radio, that is of course even better, but the longer the wavelength, the more satisfactory the radio reception will be. Why don't all amateurs connect the old parts to try it out? Finally, the author said again that whether the ground wire design is excellent has a great relationship with the transmitting range of the transmitter and the receiving range of the radio. Please pay attention to it.

Effective Filtering Device 231

— Lu Guizhen

Circuit Description: This filter is a combination of parallel resonance and series resonance methods, so its effectiveness is quite high. Its principle: the filter composed of LL1C resonates first, blocking the passage of the required frequency current. At the same time, the filter composed of C1L2 also resonates, making the required frequency current flow unhindered. Because the required frequency current has a large return resistance in the former circuit and a small return resistance in the latter, it can only choose the easier path.

Installation: LL1 is a mutual inductance coil. Use No. 30 enameled wire to wind 96 turns on a 1 and a half inch diameter tube to make LI, wind L for 15 turns at a distance of 2 points. C is a 0.00035 MFD variable capacitor. L2 is a self-inductance coil, which can be obtained by winding 60 turns of No. 30漆 on a 1 and a half inch tube. C1 is a 0.00025 MFD variable capacitor. The positions of LL1 and L2 should be at right angles to avoid coordination.

Effect: This filter can be used with any radio with low selectivity. Its adjustment method is quite easy: first apply C1 to the maximum capacity, then turn the variable capacitor of the radio to the required frequency, and then calibrate C to the same wavelength. If the selectivity is still not satisfactory, C1 can be slightly turned out, and then re-calibrate the other capacitors until satisfactory.
